Is Disney FastPass+ service offered for the attractions at 
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.Disney FastPass+,  service is currently offered on Millennium Falcon, : Smugglers Run, . However, it is not available for Star Wars, : Rise of the Resistance, . We will continually evaluate our operations and services in order to help provide a great Guest experience.Learn more about Star Wars, : Galaxy’s Edge.Star Wars, : Rise of the Resistance, While Disney FastPass+ service is not offered for Star Wars, : Rise of the Resistance, , you may be required to join a virtual queue to access the attraction.Learn more about the virtual queue for Star Wars, : Rise of the Resistance.
Is 
Star Wars, : Galaxy’s Edge,  is available during , Extra Magic Hours,  at , Disney's Hollywood Studios, —but the new Star Wars, : Rise of the Resistance,  attraction is not included at this time.Extra Magic Hours is a benefit for Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels,  and other select hotels. During Extra Magic Hours, one of the Walt Disney World theme parks opens early or closes later to allow eligible Guests to enjoy select attractions.Valid theme park admission and hotel ID is required.Learn more about Star Wars, : Galaxy’s Edge.

How much does it cost to park at Disney Springs at Walt Disney World Resort? 
Self-parking in our surface parking lots and parking garages is complimentary...Valet parking is available in the following 3 areas:Near the entrance to the Orange Garage from 10:00 AM to 2:00 AM, On West Side in front of Cirque du Soleil from 4:00 PM to 2:00 AM, In the Lemon Lot near the World of Disney shop from 10:00 AM to 2:00 AM, The cost of valet parking is $20 and will be collected at the time of pick-up. Gratuity is not included.Staying at a Walt Disney World Resort hotel? Take advantage of complimentary transportation by bus or boat. Many area accommodations also provide or arrange transportation to and from Disney Springs.

How much does it cost to park at the parks?
Check out the variety of parking options―including parking at the theme parks―available throughout Walt Disney World Resort.The rate depends on your vehicle type, but each theme park lot charges the same rate per day. Once you pay for the day, you may park at any of the other theme parks.If you are a Guest staying at a Disney Resort hotel, , you receive complimentary standard parking at Disney theme parks for the length of your Resort stay. You must present valid Disney Resort hotel identification to enter the parking lots. Complimentary standard theme park parking is also included with select annual passes.Prices subject to change without notice.
I will be visiting multiple Disney theme parks on the same day. Do I have to pay for parking at each theme park?
No. If you pay for parking at one Disney theme park, you may park at other Disney theme parks on the same day for no additional charge.If your ticket has the Park Hopper Option, you can also use the complimentary Walt Disney World transportation system,  to visit our other theme parks.If you are a Guest staying at a Disney Resort hotel, , you receive complimentary standard parking at Disney theme parks for the length of your Resort hotel stay. You must present valid Disney Resort hotel identification to enter the parking lots.Standard theme park parking is also complimentary with select Annual Passes.Check out the variety of parking options available throughout Walt Disney World Resort.
How do I get from the airport to my Disney Resort hotel?
Your best option to get to select Disney Resort hotels,  from the Orlando International Airport is via Disney's Magical Express transportation, . Disney’s Magical Express transportation is a complimentary roundtrip service that whisks you and your luggage between Orlando International Airport and select Disney Resort hotels via a deluxe motorcoach.If you did not select Disney’s Magical Express transportation and include your flight information when you made your reservation, please contact the booking agent for your Disney Resort hotel reservation.Other options include:Car Rental , Alamo® Rent A Car, the Official Rental Car of Walt Disney World Resort, has locations at the Orlando International Airport and at the Car Care Center near the parking exit of Magic Kingdom Park, . For Emerald Club customers, National Car Rental® also has a location at the Car Care Center. Shuttle service to and from your Disney Resort hotel is provided 7 days a week, Monday through Friday from 6:00 AM to 8:00 PM and Saturday and Sunday from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM. Holiday hours may vary. Shuttle service should be scheduled at least 1 hour in advance.From the United States and Canada, call (407) 824-3470. , From the United Kingdom, call 0870 400 4562.Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. Limousine Service, To make arrangements for Limousine or Town Car Service, please contact Star Transportation.From the United States and Canada, call (407) 888-5530.From the United Kingdom, call 001-407-888-5530.Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. Airport Shuttle, Mears Airport Shuttle provides transportation from Orlando International Airport to Disney Resort hotels. Tickets may be purchased when you board the shuttle. To return to Orlando International Airport, catch the shuttle near the lobby of your Disney Resort hotel. Make reservations 24 hours in advance of your return trip to the airport and allow a minimum of 2 hours before flight time.  From the United States and Canada, call (407) 423-5566.From the United Kingdom, call 0870 400 4562.Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. 
Is complimentary transportation available from Orlando International Airport to my Disney Resort hotel?
Yes. When staying at a Disney Resort hotel, , you may enjoy access to Disney's Magical Express, —a complimentary roundtrip service that whisks you and your luggage between Orlando International Airport and select Disney Resort hotels via a deluxe motorcoach. If you did not select Disney’s Magical Express and include your flight information when you made your reservation, please contact the booking agent for your Disney Resort hotel reservation.

Is there a complimentary shuttle to attractions outside of Walt Disney World Resort?
No. Walt Disney World Resort features an extensive transportation system,  to get you around the Disney theme parks, water parks and other Walt Disney World destinations. Disney’s Magical Express transportation,  is also available to transport registered Guests at select Walt Disney World Resort hotels,  to and from Orlando International Airport.If you wish to visit attractions outside of Walt Disney World Resort, we recommend that you rent a car or arrange for other transportation. The valet at your Disney Resort hotel is happy to arrange for a taxi cab to pick you up and take you wherever you wish.
Which Walt Disney World golf course is most appropriate for my skill level? 
Our 3 golf courses are 18-hole championship layouts playing to a par of 72. Each of these courses is suitable for golfers of all skill levels:Disney's Magnolia Golf Course, Disney's Palm Golf Course, Disney's Lake Buena Vista Golf Course, For less-skilled golfers who are still learning to play or families with young children, we recommend our 9-hole walking course, Disney′s Oak Trail Golf Course.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.

Where do the monorails go at Walt Disney World Resort?
Our iconic monorail is a fast—and fun—way to get around Walt Disney World Resort. There are 2 different monorail routes.The first route makes stops at the following locations:Magic Kingdom park, Disney’s Contemporary Resort, Transportation and Ticket Center (adjacent to Magic Kingdom parking), Disney's Polynesian Village Resort, Disney's Grand Floridian Resort & Spa, Please note that the above route has 2 lines. The Magic Kingdom line shuttles between Magic Kingdom park and the Transportation and Ticket Center. The Resort Hotels line stops at all of the above locations.The second monorail route stops at 2 locations:Transportation and Ticket Center, Epcot, Other popular destinations can be reached through the Walt Disney World transportation network of boats and buses. Guests have complimentary access to monorails, buses and boats at Walt Disney World Resort. 
How early and how late do the buses run between the parks and my Walt Disney Resort hotel?
Our complimentary Resort transportation—including buses, monorails and boats—generally operate from 45 minutes before a theme park’s opening time until one hour after a theme park’s closing time.Please remember that the theme park hours often vary daily and are different from park to park, so the transportation hours for each individual park will vary on any given day. If you have questions about the specific times that buses are available, please ask a Cast Member.In addition to theme park transportation, buses generally operate until 2:00 AM between Disney Resort hotels,  and , Disney Springs, . Taxi cabs are also available if you need to get around outside of our complimentary transportation hours.Learn more about Walt Disney World Resort transportation,  or view Disney theme park hours.

What services are available for Guests unable to tolerate long waits at attractions due to their disabilities?
Walt Disney World theme parks provide numerous accommodations for Guests with disabilities, including our Disability Access Service.The Disability Access Service allows Guests with disabilities—as well as an allotted number of people from his or her party—to schedule a return time at a specific attraction that is comparable to the wait time when they first arrive at that attraction.For more information, guests should visit the Guest Relations Lobby located near the entrance of each of the four theme parks.To learn more about the Disability Access Service, please download the official guide in PDF format.Please Check Our Property Rules, We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort property rules,  before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions. We regularly update our property rules to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience at Walt Disney World Resort.
What accommodations exist for Guests with disabilities at Disney’s Animal Kingdom Park?
Walt Disney World Resort theme parks provide numerous accommodations for Guests with mobility disabilities, Guests with visual disabilities,  and Guests with hearing disabilities.Some examples of accommodations that we offer include:Rental wheelchairs, Rental electric conveyance vehicles (ECVs), Accommodations for service animals, Assistive Listening systems, Reflective Captioning, Sign Language interpretation, Text Typewriter telephones, Handheld Captioning, Video Captioning, Audio Description devices, Braille guidebooks, Digital audio tours, Learn more about accommodations for Guests with disabilities at Disney's Animal Kingdom Park.
What accommodations exist for Guests with disabilities at Disney's Blizzard Beach Water Park?
Walt Disney World Resort water parks provide numerous accommodations for Guests with mobility disabilities, Guests with visual disabilities,  and Guests with hearing disabilities.Some examples of accommodations that we offer include:Accommodations for service animals, Wheelchair rentals, Assistive Listening systems, Reflective Captioning, Sign Language interpretation, Text Typewriter telephones, Handheld Captioning, Video Captioning, Audio Description devices, Braille guidebooks, Digital audio tours, Learn more about accommodations for Guests with disabilities at Disney's Blizzard Beach Water Park.
What accommodations exist for Guests with cognitive disabilities?
Walt Disney World Resort provides numerous accommodations for Guests with cognitive disabilities such as Autism Spectrum Disorder.Some examples of available accommodations include Rider Switch, Disability Access Service and break areas for Guests who become over-stimulated. We also offer an assortment of tips and suggestions to help plan a successful day in the theme parks.Learn more about accommodations for Guests with cognitive disabilities at Walt Disney World Resort.

Can I rent a wheelchair or ECV during my visit to Walt Disney World Resort? 
Yes. Can I use my own wheelchair in the theme parks?
Yes. You may use your own wheelchair at all Walt Disney World theme parks. I have questions or comments about accessibility on disneyworld.com for Guests with visual impairments. Who should I contact?
We have affirmed the importance of making our theme park and cruise line websites accessible to all Guests, including those with visual impairments. If you have any questions or comments regarding website accessibility, please e-mail us.
How do I book a Disney Resort hotel room for a Guest with a disability?
You have the option of filtering by “Accessible Rooms” when you book your Walt Disney World vacation online.If you would like to discuss accommodations for a specific disability, please call (407) 939-7675. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Learn more about accommodations for Guests with disabilities at Walt Disney World Resort hotels.
Does the Walt Disney World Resort bus transportation system accommodate wheelchairs?
Yes. The complimentary Walt Disney World Resort bus transportation system does accommodate wheelchairs. To help us plan ahead, please indicate that you will be traveling with a wheelchair when you book your vacation.Learn more about how Walt Disney World Resort can help accommodate Guests with mobility disabilities.
If I rent a wheelchair or ECV, do I get to keep it for my entire stay?
Wheelchairs and Electric Conveyance Vehicles (ECVs) rented at most Walt Disney World destinations, —including our theme parks, water parks and Disney Springs, —are only for one specific location and must be returned before exiting.Length-of-stay rental tickets are available for a one-time payment, but wheelchairs or ECVs must still be returned before exiting each location.In addition to our theme parks, water parks and Disney Springs, there are also a limited number of wheelchairs available for rental at select Disney Resort hotels; these rentals can be kept for your entire stay.Before your next visit, be sure to learn more about wheelchair rentals,  or ECV rentals.
What is the street address of my Disney Resort hotel?
The street address appears on the web page for each hotel. View a complete list of all of the Disney Resort hotels. Select your Resort hotel to see the street address.
I’m on my way to—or already at—my Resort hotel but haven’t checked in yet. Can I still participate in the Direct-to-Room service?
Yes. You can use the Direct-to-Room service anytime in advance up to and including your arrival day. However, we recommend starting the check-in process before your arrival day so you can make your vacation experience even easier and more convenient.Check-in time for all Disney Resort hotels is 3:00 PM, except for Disney Deluxe Villa Resorts, which have a check-in time of 4:00 PM.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
Can I extend my balance due date on a vacation package?
No. Balance due dates cannot be extended for vacation packages.If you wish to cancel an existing reservation for which you have already applied payment, call (407) 939-4357. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.You can view your existing Disney Resort hotel reservations on the My Reservations page in My Disney Experience, . You will have to sign in to view your reservations.
I have an existing package or hotel reservation and I have only paid my deposit. Will you automatically deduct the balance due payment from my credit card?
No. We will not automatically charge your credit card to pay the balance due.If you have a vacation package, you can pay off the balance online,  or call (407) 939-7675. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. For your convenience, you are able to use the payment method stored in your online account.If you have a room-only reservation, you will pay off your balance when you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel.You can view your existing Disney Resort hotel reservations on the My Reservations page in My Disney Experience, . You will have to sign in to view your reservations.
Will you send me any reminders regarding the balance due on my hotel or package reservation?
Yes. We will send a notice by email or direct mail when your final payment is past due.If you have a vacation package, you can pay off the balance online,  or call (407) 939-7675. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.If you have a room-only reservation, you will pay off your balance when you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel.You can view your existing Disney Resort hotel reservations on the My Reservtions page in My Disney Experience, . You will have to sign in to view your reservations.
What are the benefits of the Direct-to-Room service?
The Direct-to-Room service lets you...View your reservation, Simplify your arrival, Bypass the Front Desk⁠, Receive real-time room ready updates, including room number and arrival instructions, Have digital access to Resort hotel maps, Use your MagicBand or the My Disney Experience app to unlock your door, Begin the fun and magic of your vacation even sooner, Need anything else? You can still visit the Front Desk any time after you've arrived!, Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
Is breakfast included in my Disney Resort hotel room reservation?
No. However, you should be able to find a dining location offering breakfast at your Disney Resort hotel. , Disney dining plans,  are also available as an option to Disney Resort Hotel Packages, , and many of these convenient plans do include breakfast options. , View a complete list of the Disney Resort hotels at Walt Disney World Resort.
How do I cancel my hotel reservation?
Depending on the type of reservation, you will either be able to cancel the reservation online or you will need to call the Disney Reservation Center for assistance.Sign in to your Disney Account and go to My Reservations, , where you will see the reservation listed. If your reservation can be canceled online, you’ll see a link for “Cancel Reservation.”, If your reservation can only be canceled by phone, you’ll see a message indicating you need to call (407) 934-7639. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.Please note that a cancelation fee may apply.View your Disney Resort hotel, dining reservations, tickets and other plans.
How do I update or modify a hotel or package reservation?
Depending on the type of reservation, you may be able to update or modify your hotel or package reservation online. Simply sign in to your Disney Account,  and go to My Reservations, , where you’ll see a link for “Modify Reservation.”, If your reservation cannot be updated or modified online, please call (407) 934-7639. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permissions to call.Please note that a change fee may apply.
What are the Disney Resort hotel check-in and check-out times?
The check-in time is 4:00 PM for Disney Deluxe Villas, 3:00 PM for the other Disney Resort hotels. The check-out time is 11:00 AM. , When you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel, visit the Front Desk and we’ll provide any theme park tickets that are included in your Disney Resort Hotel Package—even if it is before the standard check-in time.Plus, if you take advantage of Disney′s Magical Express transportation, , we can deliver your luggage directly to your room when it is available, so you are free to start enjoying Walt Disney World Resort. Only select Disney Resort hotels,  offer access to Disney’s Magical Express transportation. , If you're using the Direct-to-Room service, you can use your MagicBand or the Unlock Door feature on the My Disney Experience app to begin enjoying your Disney Resort hotel in certain areas—such as the pool—on the day of your scheduled arrival, even before your room is ready. You can also continue to use the Resort hotel facilities for the rest of the day after you check out.View a complete list of the Disney Resort hotels at Walt Disney World Resort.
Can I use the Direct-to-Room service if I’m staying in a Club-Level room?
Absolutely! The Direct-to-Room service is available for all room types at participating Disney Resort hotels.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
Is there a complimentary shuttle to attractions outside of Walt Disney World Resort?
No. Walt Disney World Resort features an extensive transportation system,  to get you around the Disney theme parks, water parks and other Walt Disney World destinations. Disney’s Magical Express transportation,  is also available to transport registered Guests at select Walt Disney World Resort hotels,  to and from Orlando International Airport.If you wish to visit attractions outside of Walt Disney World Resort, we recommend that you rent a car or arrange for other transportation. The valet at your Disney Resort hotel is happy to arrange for a taxi cab to pick you up and take you wherever you wish.
Where can I find my hotel or package reservation confirmation number?
View an existing reservation online on the My Reservations page in My Disney Experience,  to check the confirmation number. You will need to sign into your account.When you make a new reservation online, you will see your confirmation number on both the online confirmation page and your confirmation email. If you make your reservation over the phone, your booking agent will verbally provide you with a confirmation number—you may also receive either a confirmation email or receive a letter in the mail with the confirmation number.Please keep your confirmation number for reference. If you wish to view a reservation online that you made over the phone, you may need to link your reservation to My Disney Experience,  by entering your confirmation number and the phone number that you used to make the call. After you do so, the reservation will show up on the My Reservations page to allow you to easily reference it in the future.

Yes. What accommodations exist for Guests with disabilities at Disney’s Animal Kingdom Park?
Walt Disney World Resort theme parks provide numerous accommodations for Guests with mobility disabilities, Guests with visual disabilities,  and Guests with hearing disabilities.Some examples of accommodations that we offer include:Rental wheelchairs, Rental electric conveyance vehicles (ECVs), Accommodations for service animals, Assistive Listening systems, Reflective Captioning, Sign Language interpretation, Text Typewriter telephones, Handheld Captioning, Video Captioning, Audio Description devices, Braille guidebooks, Digital audio tours, Learn more about accommodations for Guests with disabilities at Disney's Animal Kingdom Park.

How does Walt Disney World Resort work to help the environment?
Environmentality is an attitude and a commitment to our environment, where we actively seek ways to be friendlier to our planet. We're committed to making smart choices now to preserve our world for the future. We encourage environmental awareness among our Cast Members, our Guests and our community. Is my room assigned when I initiate the Direct-to-Room service?
No. Rooms are not assigned until your arrival day. We take into consideration information you provide during the online check-in process, such as your estimated arrival time and any room location request selections (subject to availability), when assigning a room.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on,  or with the My Disney Experience app.

Are Guests permitted to have firearms, ammunition or weapons in Disney Resort hotels or Disney Vacation Club Resorts?
No. Guests are not permitted to have firearms, ammunition, knives or weapons of any kind at or in Disney Resort Hotels,  and Disney Vacation Club Resorts, , including in hotel rooms, units, vacation home villas and general public areas within the hotels and resorts.

How does Online Check-In work? 
When you use Online Check-In, , you provide us in advance of your arrival with the information that we typically collect at the Front Desk during the standard check-in process. Upon arrival at your Disney Resort hotel, you will visit a specially designated Front Desk location where we’ll give you a Welcome Folder and your MagicBand.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using Online Check-In on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
What benefits do I receive with my room-only reservation at a Disney Resort hotel?
A room-only reservation not only includes a stay at a comfortable Disney Resort hotel, but it also provides additional perks, such as complimentary usage of the Walt Disney World transportation system,  and access to complimentary Disney’s Magical Express transportation,  to and from Orlando International Airport.Extra Magic Hours, You may be able to take advantage of the Extra Magic Hours benefit,  offered select nights at our theme parks. A park reservation and valid admission for the same park on the same date and Resort ID are required. To see when and where the Extra Magic Hours benefit is offered, or view today’s park hours. The Extra Magic Hours benefit is temporarily suspended.Plan Ahead with FastPass+, Guests staying at a Disney Resort hotel with valid theme park admission can also make FastPass+ selections,  up to 60 days before their check-in. As a result of the COVID-19 impact, FastPass+ service will be temporarily suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to manage capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing.Interested in Vacation Packages?, If you are interested in theme park tickets and a Disney dining plan, a Disney Resort Hotel Package,  might be a great option for you. As a result of physical distancing, the capacity in restaurants and the availability of dining experiences are very limited and certain experiences such as Character Dining cannot be provided. As a result, Disney dining plans are temporarily unavailable.View a complete list of the Disney Resort hotels at Walt Disney World Resort.
When I use the Direct-to-Room service, what sort of information do I need to provide online?
During the online check-in process, you’ll provide the same information you would typically provide to the Front Desk during a standard check-in—including a credit card for incidental charges, your arrival time, room location requests (which are subject to availability), home address and mobile phone number. We’ll also ask you to create a 4-digit personal identification number that you—and the other members of your party with charging privileges—will use to verify your identity when you make purchases and use dining entitlements at Walt Disney World Resort.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.

What is the Online Check-in Service?
The Online Check-in service is a convenient option that starts your check-in process online. As a component of the Direct-to-Room service, , Online Check-in can help Disney Resort hotel,  Guests reduce registration time and simplify their arrival—while still enjoying a magical Disney welcome.When you use the Direct-to-Room service, you provide us in advance of your arrival with information typically collected during a traditional check-in at the Front Desk. On arrival day, you’ll receive notifications on your mobile device (based on communication preferences you have opted into) with real-time updates, including when your room is ready and what your room number is. When your room is ready, use the Resort hotel map in the app to find your room. Then unlock your door with your MagicBand, or use the Unlock Door feature on the app.Begin your check-in to go directly to your room by linking your Disney Resort hotel reservation,  to your Disney Account. Once linked, view your reservation on the “My Plans”,  page and select “Start Check-in.” Or view your reservation from the “My Plans” screen in the My Disney Experience app.

What kind of identification do I need to supply if I wish to enjoy an alcoholic beverage during my visit?
Alcoholic beverages can be purchased at Walt Disney World Resort by all Guests 21 years of age or older.Any Guest who wishes to purchase an alcoholic beverage at Walt Disney World Resort must present one of the following valid forms of identification:U.S. state driver’s license (includes U.S. territories*), U.S. state ID (includes U.S. territories*), U.S. military ID, Original passport, Copy of passport (either on paper or captured on a mobile device), along with a government-issued photo ID** that can verify the person and birth date shown on the copy, NEXUS card issued by U.S. Customs and Border Patrol (Canadian Guests only), All Guests visiting from outside of the United States are required to present both a valid passport as well as another form of government-issued photo ID from their country of origin.For all questions concerning our identification requirements, please call (407) 939-6244. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Walt Disney World Resort reserves the right to refuse sale and/or service of alcoholic beverages to anyone.The Walt Disney World Resort alcohol policy is subject to change without notice.*U.S. territories include Puerto Rico, Guam, Northern Mariana Islands, U.S. Virgin Islands and American Samoa.**Foreign driver’s licenses or ID cards are not acceptable by themselves.

How do I view my existing hotel reservation?
View an existing Disney Resort hotel reservation on the My Reservations page in My Disney Experience. You will have to sign in to view your reservation.If you’ve visited the above page, but you still don’t see your reservation, you may have to link it to your disneyworld.com account, . You will need your Resort Confirmation Number.If you continue to have problems finding a reservation, please call (407) 939-4357. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
I arrived early, but my room's not ready yet. What can I do?
No worries! You can use your MagicBand or the Unlock Door feature on the My Disney Experience app,  to enjoy your Disney Resort hotel in a variety of areas—including the swimming pool—before your room is available.Have luggage? Drop it off with Valet, Bell Service or Luggage Assistance at the entrance of your Resort for storage until your room is ready.If you take advantage of Disney′s Magical Express transportation, , we can deliver your luggage directly to your room when it is available, so you are free to start enjoying Walt Disney World Resort. Only select Disney Resort hotels,  offer access to Disney’s Magical Express transportation.If you have a Disney dining plan, you can start using it the day you’re scheduled to arrive even before your room is available. Feel free to take advantage of quick-service locations in the hotel to utilize entitlements of the plan, such as getting a refillable drink mug, snack or a meal. To redeem, Guests need to show their MagicBand or card. If you don’t have a MagicBand, but have one awaiting your pickup at the Front Desk of your Disney Resort hotel, you can retrieve it at your convenience.*, Check-in time for all Disney Resort hotels is 3:00 PM, except for Disney Deluxe Villa Resorts, which have a check-in time of 4:00 PM. The checkout time is 11:00 AM.* Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.
Why have you updated your rules and policies?
These updates are intended to provide a more enjoyable experience for everyone who visits by, among other things, easing guest flow and reducing congestion.What is changing?, For a complete list of property rules, please visit Disneyworld.com/rules.Key policy changes, which are designed to, among other things, help improve guest flow, ease congestion and make the park experience more enjoyable for everyone who visits include:Smoking areas will no longer be present in our domestic theme parks, water parks and ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex. Guests may use designated smoking areas outside of the parks, at Disney Resort hotels and at Disney Springs.Strollers must be 31” (79cm) wide and 52” (132cm) long or smaller.As a reminder, wagons are not permitted in our parks. Stroller wagons will also no longer be permitted.Loose and dry ice is not permitted in our parks. Reusable ice packs are recommended.Why is smoking no longer allowed at Walt Disney World Resort theme parks, water parks and ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex?, Walt Disney World Resort makes updates from time to time and the removal of smoking areas is intended to provide a more enjoyable experience for everyone who visits.Are electronic cigarettes and vaping permitted at Walt Disney World Resort?, Smoking and vaping are only permitted in designated smoking areas.Where can guests smoke?, Guests may smoke in designated areas located outside the park entry points and in specified areas at Disney Resort hotels and Disney Springs. , Why are you reducing the size of strollers and prohibiting wagons in your theme parks and water parks?, Walt Disney World Resort makes updates from time to time, and the reduction of stroller sizes is intended to ease guest flow and reduce congestion, making the park experience more enjoyable for everyone who visits. Many strollers, including many double jogging strollers, fit within these guidelines.Are stroller-wagons permitted?, Stroller wagons, whether pushed or pulled, will not be permitted at any theme park or water park or at indoor venues at ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex.What if my stroller is larger than the size allowed?, Strollers are available for rent at the parks. Guests who have additional questions on the stroller policy may visit Guest Relations for more information.How do I ensure my stroller falls within the size guidelines?, Strollers should be no larger than 31” (79 cm) wide and 52” (132cm) long when measured across the widest and longest points.Why is loose or dry ice not permitted in your parks?, In order to improve guest flow, ease congestion and streamline the bag-check and entry processes, loose and dry ice is not permitted. Reusable ice packs are recommended.What happens if I need ice for baby food, medicine, or some other item?, Reusable ice packs are recommended. Cups of ice are available at no charge at Food & Beverage locations.Where can guests with disabilities find more information on the rule and policy updates?, Nothing has changed about how we make accommodations for guests with disabilities. Meeting their needs is extremely important to us. Guests with disabilities who have questions or concerns about any of the updates may visit Guest Relations or contact Disability.Services@DisneyParks.com,  or 407-560-2547 to address their needs.
What security measures do you have in place?
We have a comprehensive approach to security that includes measures that are visible and others that are not, including the presence of uniformed police officers. We do not broadly discuss the specifics of our security procedures to avoid compromising their effectiveness.
What areas of Walt Disney World Resort permit smoking?
Walt Disney World theme parks, water parks, ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex and Disney resort hotels are smoke-free environments except for designated smoking areas.At Disney Resort hotels, , smoking is permitted in designated outdoor smoking areas. Smoking is not permitted in guest rooms or on balconies. Guests can request location information at the hotel Front Desk.If you have questions about our smoking policy or wish to locate the nearest designated smoking area, please visit our Designated Smoking Areas page,  or ask a Disney Cast Member.Marijuana, Smoking marijuana is not permitted at any time in Disney Resort hotels, even in designated smoking areas.Please Check Our Walt Disney World Resort Rules, We regularly update our Walt Disney World Resort Rules,  to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience. We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort Rules before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions.
Can I smoke on the patio or balcony of my Disney Resort hotel room?
No. Guests may not smoke in their Disney Resort hotel rooms, on patios or on balconies. Each Disney Resort hotel features designated outdoor smoking areas.If you have questions about our smoking policy or wish to locate the nearest designated smoking area, please visit our Designated Smoking Areas page,  or ask a Disney Cast Member.View a complete list of the Disney Resort hotels at Walt Disney World Resort.
How is the Disney Resort hotel smoke-free policy enforced?
To cover the costs of cleaning and restoring the room to a smoke-free condition, a US $250 to US $500 room recovery fee plus tax (based on the Disney Resort hotel and room type) will be charged to Guests who smoke in hotel rooms, on balconies or on patios.Each Disney Resort hotel features designated outdoor smoking areas. The Concierge and Front Desk are available to direct you to the nearest smoking location.View a complete list of the Disney Resort hotels at Walt Disney World Resort.

Can I view a package or hotel reservation booked by my travel agent?
Yes. To do so, you must first link the reservation with your Disney account, . You will have to sign in to your account,  to view My Reservations.If you continue to have problems finding your reservation, please contact your travel professional.

Can Disney Vacation Club Members use the Direct-to-Room service when using Vacation Points or cash reservations?

Does the Walt Disney World Resort bus transportation system accommodate wheelchairs?
Yes. The complimentary Walt Disney World Resort bus transportation system does accommodate wheelchairs. To help us plan ahead, please indicate that you will be traveling with a wheelchair when you book your vacation.Learn more about how Walt Disney World Resort can help accommodate Guests with mobility disabilities.
If I rent a wheelchair or ECV, do I get to keep it for my entire stay?
Wheelchairs and Electric Conveyance Vehicles (ECVs) rented at most Walt Disney World destinations, —including our theme parks, water parks and Disney Springs, —are only for one specific location and must be returned before exiting.Length-of-stay rental tickets are available for a one-time payment, but wheelchairs or ECVs must still be returned before exiting each location.In addition to our theme parks, water parks and Disney Springs, there are also a limited number of wheelchairs available for rental at select Disney Resort hotels; these rentals can be kept for your entire stay.Before your next visit, be sure to learn more about wheelchair rentals,  or ECV rentals.
What is a Disney dining plan and how does it work?
Disney dining plans are a convenient and flexible way to enjoy meals and snacks at many of the restaurants and food service locations at Walt Disney World Resort. Dining plans are included in some Disney Resort Hotel Packages, —which also include a Resort hotel stay and theme park tickets.Learn more about Disney dining plans—including the detail about how each plan works.
Are Disney dining plans available separately from vacation packages?
No. Disney dining plans are only available as part of Disney Resort Hotel Packages, —which also include a Resort hotel stay and theme park tickets.Learn more about Disney Dining Plans.
Are gratuities included with dining plans?
No. Gratuities are not included with packages that include dining plans—unless otherwise indicated.An automatic 18% gratuity charge will be added to your bill for parties of 6 or more. Merchandise or photo-imaging products that may be offered at Character Dining experiences are also not included, except at Cinderella′s Royal Table,  and Akershus Royal Banquet Hall.
How do I determine how many meals and snacks I have left on my dining plan? 
Your dining plan includes a certain number of meal and snack entitlements. The amount of entitlements required for a meal or snack varies based on your specific dining plan and the restaurant and food service locations where you dine.After you dine at a table-service restaurant, your party’s remaining entitlements will be printed on the receipt. Ask your hotel Concierge for a complete printout of your meals used and available.You can also view your remaining entitlements when placing a mobile order on the My Disney Experience app. Learn more about our Disney dining plans.
Do I have to purchase a vacation package to select a Disney dining plan?
Yes. Disney dining plans can only be purchased as part of a Disney Resort Package, , making them flexible and convenient ways to enjoy your Walt Disney World vacation.
How do I make dining reservations for my Disney dining plan?
While all of our dining plans are flexible, your dining plan entitlements are only valid at select Walt Disney World restaurants and food service locations.When you book your reservations online, , you have the option to only show restaurants that participate in a Disney dining plan. Before you confirm your reservation, please double check to ensure that the location accepts your specific dining plan.Learn more about Disney dining plans—including available dining locations for each plan.
What is considered a dining plan snack?
The details about what is considered a snack—and where they are available—are specific to your dining plan. Learn more about Disney dining plans—including the details of each plan.
What kinds of prices can I expect to pay for food inside the theme parks and at Disney Resort hotels?
Costs will vary from location to location, and are all listed online. Each spot has ranked according to price using an easy-to-follow, dollar sign breakdown:$ ($14.99 and under per adult), $$ ($15 to $34.99 per adult), $$$ ($35 to $59.99 per adult), $$$$ (over $60 per adult), Range reflects the average price of adult dinner entrées (breakfast and lunch generally cost less), except Character Dining locations, buffet locations, dinner shows, and special dining events where range reflects the average adult price of entire meal and non-alcoholic beverages. Range excludes alcoholic beverages, taxes and gratuities except at dinner shows where beer and wine, taxes and gratuities are included.
What is Disney Check and what does the Disney Check symbol mean on menus at Walt Disney World restaurants?
Disney Check makes it easy to spot food and beverage choices that fit your family’s healthy lifestyle. When you see Disney Check, you'll know that the food you're looking at is tasty and meets Disney nutritional guidelines!, You can find the Disney Check icon next to specific items on Walt Disney World restaurant,  menus and Disneyland Resort restaurant,  menus—including the online menus found on disneyworld.com,  and disneyland.com,  restaurant pages. In addition, you’ll find Disney Check on various Disney-licensed food products sold at grocery stores across the country and at some of your favorite retail and food-related websites.Learn more about the Disney Check—including specific nutrition guideline information for all food categories.
Which Walt Disney World restaurants take reservations?
Select restaurants at our 4 theme parks, Disney Resort hotels and Disney Springs take reservations. In addition, select dinner shows and special dining events also take reservations. Why is a credit card required to make a dining reservation?
We require your credit card to make a dining reservation and use it as a place holder.Your credit card won’t be charged before you dine with us unless you either don’t show up for your reservation or cancel after 11:59 PM Eastern Time on the day before your arrival. So, we encourage you to keep your reservation and enjoy your dining experience!, For more convenience, add a credit card to your profile. That makes the process of booking reservations proceed even more quickly for you.

Are halal meals available at Walt Disney World Resort?
Yes. Halal meals can be accommodated at select restaurants and should be requested at least 24 hours in advance. A halal meal can be requested when making your reservation at a table service restaurant by calling (407) 824-1391. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. For all other restaurants, email Special.Diets@DisneyWorld.com, . Also be sure to indicate any dietary requirements upon arrival at your dining location. Please know there may be a higher wait time due to the special care we take to provide a halal meal. Halal meat options will vary at all locations and in some cases only vegetarian or specific seafood meals will be available.
Can food products from home be prepared by Disney chefs or Cast Members?
No. Our chefs and other Cast Members may not prepare, cook, heat or reheat any food items brought in by our Guests.However, if you have special dietary requests, we will work with you to try and meet your needs. Learn more about Special Dietary Requests. 
Are kosher meals available at Walt Disney World Resort?
Yes. Kosher meals can be accommodated at all table-service and select quick-service restaurants. Kosher meals should be requested 24 hours in advance by calling (407) 824-1391. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. Also be sure to indicate any dietary requirements upon arrival at your dining location. Please know there may be a higher wait time due to the special care we take to provide a kosher meal.
Where can I find Disney Characters?
One of the best ways to see Disney Characters is to make reservations at a restaurant with Character Dining. Character Dining meals are very popular, so book your reservations early!, Theme parks are also home to attractions,  and entertainment,  that feature Disney Characters. Plus, you never know who you might find when you visit the parks—check the printed Guidemap for additional Character Greeting locations.
Why don’t some of my dining reservations appear in the My Plans or My Reservations sections of My Disney Experience?
Your dining reservations are tied to a specific Disney account. It is possible that you made the reservation on another account or you were not signed in when you made the reservations. They also might not be showing up if you made your reservations over the phone, at the hotel concierge or in person at the restaurant.Link an existing dining reservation to your Disney account, . You will have to sign in to link the reservation.If you are still unable to see your dining reservations, please call (407) 939-3463. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
Can I book more than one reservation for the same meal period?
No. Guests are not permitted to book dining reservations within 2 hours of another reservation. This constraint helps us provide you with the most choices and availability when making your dining plans.Other Important Details, Reservation availability for select Walt Disney World restaurants typically begins each day at approximately 5:45 AM.Please be aware that if you cancel a restaurant reservation, your previously scheduled reservation time will immediately be made available to another Guest.All newly introduced dining events—such as special dining experiences and dessert parties—can typically be booked beginning at 7:00 AM on the day their offers become available.
What is a quick-service restaurant?
A Walt Disney World quick-service restaurant offers great food and fast service. They are generally either cafeteria-style or counter-service venues. You order or take the food items that you want, pay for your food and sit down to enjoy your meal.In addition to quick-service restaurants, Walt Disney World Resort features a diverse selection of casual dining and fine dining restaurants that offer sit-down meals with table service. Most casual dining and fine dining restaurants take reservations, , but quick-service restaurants do not.View all quick-service restaurants.
What kind of identification do I need to supply if I wish to enjoy an alcoholic beverage during my visit?
Alcoholic beverages can be purchased at Walt Disney World Resort by all Guests 21 years of age or older.Any Guest who wishes to purchase an alcoholic beverage at Walt Disney World Resort must present one of the following valid forms of identification:U.S. state driver’s license (includes U.S. territories*), U.S. state ID (includes U.S. territories*), U.S. military ID, Original passport, Copy of passport (either on paper or captured on a mobile device), along with a government-issued photo ID** that can verify the person and birth date shown on the copy, NEXUS card issued by U.S. Customs and Border Patrol (Canadian Guests only), All Guests visiting from outside of the United States are required to present both a valid passport as well as another form of government-issued photo ID from their country of origin.For all questions concerning our identification requirements, please call (407) 939-6244. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Walt Disney World Resort reserves the right to refuse sale and/or service of alcoholic beverages to anyone.The Walt Disney World Resort alcohol policy is subject to change without notice.*U.S. territories include Puerto Rico, Guam, Northern Mariana Islands, U.S. Virgin Islands and American Samoa.**Foreign driver’s licenses or ID cards are not acceptable by themselves.

Do your restaurants have plant-based options?
Yes! Our plant-based options are made with no animal meat, dairy, eggs or honey. They are made with ingredients that come from plants, including grains, vegetables, fruits, nuts, seeds and legumes. Plant-based items will be noted with a green leaf icon on dining menus beginning on October 1, 2019 at quick-service locations and October 3, 2019 for table-service locations.We’ve found that many of our vegetarian and vegan guests tailor their diet to their lifestyle and their dietary preferences may vary. While we do not have separate kitchens to prepare plant-based menu items, we make reasonable efforts to avoid cross-contact. If you have questions about specific ingredients, menu items, or shared surfaces or equipment, one of our Cast Members will be happy to help.
How do I take advantage of Extra Magic Hours?
The Extra Magic Hours benefit,  allows registered Guests—with valid theme park admission—of Disney Resort hotels, Walt Disney World Swan Hotel, Walt Disney World Dolphin Hotel,  and Shades of Green® Resort,  to experience select attractions at the theme parks before or after the parks are open to the general public. Disney Golden Oak Residents or Guests of Disney Golden Oak Residents may also take advantage of Extra Magic Hours. Times and availability varies.To take advantage of the Extra Magic Hours benefit, , each member of your party will need to present one of the following:A valid theme park ticket and MagicBand,  or Key to the World Card, A Disney Golden Oak ID card, Please Check Our Property Rules, We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort property rules,  before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions. We regularly update our property rules to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience at Walt Disney World Resort.
How can I find out the Extra Magic Hours for a theme park?
View details about Extra Magic Hours,  or on the printed Times Guide that you’ll receive when you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel, . The printed Times Guide will also contain the regular park hours for the current week.Please Check Our Property Rules, We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort property rules,  before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions. We regularly update our property rules to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience at Walt Disney World Resort.
Do I need a special ticket for Extra Magic Hours?
Any valid theme park tickets allow you to take advantage of the Extra Magic Hours benefit, . Extra Magic Hours are only available to registered Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels, Walt Disney World Swan Hotel, Walt Disney World Dolphin Hotel,  and Shades of Green® Resort, —plus Disney Golden Oak Residents or Guests of Disney Golden Oak Residents.When planning your schedule, please remember that to visit more than one theme park per day, you’ll need to purchase the Park Hopper Option or Park Hopper Plus Option on your theme park ticket—or the Ultimate Ticket Option for United Kingdom Guests.Please Check Our Property Rules, We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort property rules,  before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions. We regularly update our property rules to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience at Walt Disney World Resort.

Are maps of Walt Disney World theme parks available in advance of my visit? 
Yes. View our interactive online maps.Using advanced Google Maps technology, our interactive maps provide an overview of Walt Disney World Resort—including the theme parks, water parks, Disney Resort hotels, golf courses, attractions, shopping, dining, entertainment and Guest Services.
What information do your online maps contain?
Our interactive maps,  provide much of the information that you need to familiarize yourself with Walt Disney World Resort and plan your visit. Using advanced Google Maps technology, our interactive maps show the locations of theme parks, water parks, Disney Resort hotels, golf courses, attractions, shopping, dining, entertainment and Guest Services—including details such as ATMs, lockers and baby care centers. 
Is the Play Disney Parks mobile app the same app as the My Disney Experience app at Walt Disney World Resort?
No. The Play Disney Parks,  app is a separate, first-of-its-kind Disney app that gives Guests the chance to explore and have fun at the Walt Disney World theme parks in a whole new way.While the popular My Disney Experience,  app at Walt Disney World Resort will continue serving Guests in their vacation planning before and during their visits, the all-new Play Disney Parks app gives you even more ways to enhance the in-park experience—with in-queue games you can play while waiting in line for select attractions, interactive park experiences that brings surrounding environments to life, Disney trivia, magical achievements and much more.To learn more, download the Play Disney Parks mobile app today!, Message, data and roaming rates may apply. Availability subject to handset limitations, and features may vary by handset, service provider or otherwise. Coverage and app stores not available everywhere. Music streaming feature requires an Apple Music subscription. Separate terms and conditions apply. If you’re under 18, get your parents’ permission first. Some features require separate theme park admission.Apple, the Apple logo, iPhone and Apple Music are trademarks of Apple Inc., registered in the U.S. and other countries. Google Play is a trademark of Google LLC.
