If a hurricane warning is issued within 7 days of my arrival date and I want to cancel or reschedule my vacation, what should I do with my airline tickets? 
If you booked your air travel through the Walt Disney Travel Company and you want to reschedule, we will attempt to rebook your air travel. However, you will be responsible for any cancellation or change fees imposed by the airline. If you did not book your air travel through the Walt Disney Travel Company, you should contact your airline.
Will I be responsible for any cancellation or change fees or other amounts if a hurricane warning is issued within 7 days of my arrival date?
If a hurricane warning is issued by the National Hurricane Center for the Orlando area—or for your place of residence—within 7 days of your scheduled arrival date, you may call in advance to reschedule or cancel your Walt Disney Travel Company Magic Your Way vacation package and most room only reservations (booked directly with Disney) without any cancellation or change fees imposed by Disney.If you have products and services provided by third-party suppliers included in your vacation—such as airlines, hotels, car rental agencies or travel insurance companies—you will continue to be responsible for any non-refundable payments, as well as cancellation or change fees assessed by those suppliers. The policy does not apply to certain special events or dining experiences.This policy also applies to Disney's Vero Beach Resort,  or Disney's Hilton Head Island Resort,  in the event a hurricane warning is issued for those destinations.If you have questions or you wish to reschedule your vacation due to a hurricane warning, please call (407) 939-7675. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
A hurricane warning has been issued within 7 days of my arrival date and I did not book my package through the Walt Disney Travel Company. Does the Walt Disney Travel Company cancellation policy apply to my package too?
No. You should contact your travel agent or tour operator directly for information relating to the cancellation and change policies that apply to your package.
I received a special offer when I booked my vacation with the Walt Disney Travel Company. If a hurricane warning is issued within 7 days of my arrival date and I reschedule, will I get the same special offer?
Cast Members will be able to reschedule your vacation to your new desired travel dates if the same special offer is available. If the same special offer is not available Cast Members will assist by identifying alternate offers during your new desired travel dates. All amounts you paid to the Walt Disney Travel Company for rooms, park tickets, dining plans and other Disney products and services will be applied toward your new reservation.Any discounts or special offers applicable to your original confirmed vacation may not apply to the rescheduled vacation travel dates. You are responsible for applicable package pricing for the new vacation dates.
If a hurricane warning is issued within 7 days of my arrival date and I have a sports or group package, does the Walt Disney Travel Company hurricane cancellation policy apply to my package?
The policy only applies to Walt Disney Travel Company Magic Your Way Packages, as well as rooms and packages for sports groups.The policy does not apply to rooms or packages for youth groups, other groups and special events. It also does not apply to meetings and conventions.
What does it mean for my vacation plans if a hurricane warning is issued within 7 days of my arrival date?
If a hurricane warning is issued by the National Hurricane Center for the Orlando area—or for your place of residence—within 7 days of your scheduled arrival date, you may call in advance to reschedule or cancel your Walt Disney Travel Company Disney Resort Hotel Package and most room only reservations (booked directly with Disney) without any cancellation or change fees imposed by Disney.If you have products and services provided by third-party suppliers included in your vacation—such as airlines, hotels, car rental agencies or travel insurance companies—you will continue to be responsible for any non-refundable payments, as well as cancellation or change fees assessed by those suppliers. The policy does not apply to certain special events or dining experiences.This policy also applies to Disney's Vero Beach Resort,  or Disney's Hilton Head Island Resort,  in the event a hurricane warning is issued for those destinations.If you have questions or you wish to reschedule your vacation due to a hurricane warning, please call (407) 939-7675. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
If I reschedule my vacation to a different date because of a hurricane warning, will I be able to get my same accommodations?
If you are scheduled to arrive within 7 days of a hurricane warning, you may call us in advance to reschedule without a Disney imposed change fee. We cannot guarantee availability of similar accommodations for the new travel dates. All amounts you paid to Disney for rooms, theme park tickets, dining plans and other Disney products and services will be applied toward your new reservation.Any discounts or special offers applicable to your original confirmed vacation will not apply to the rescheduled vacation travel dates. You are responsible for applicable package pricing for the new vacation dates.The policy does not apply to certain special events and dining experiences. 
Why have you updated your rules and policies?
These updates are intended to provide a more enjoyable experience for everyone who visits by, among other things, easing guest flow and reducing congestion.What is changing?, For a complete list of property rules, please visit Disneyworld.com/rules.Key policy changes, which are designed to, among other things, help improve guest flow, ease congestion and make the park experience more enjoyable for everyone who visits include:Smoking areas will no longer be present in our domestic theme parks, water parks and ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex. Guests may use designated smoking areas outside of the parks, at Disney Resort hotels and at Disney Springs.Strollers must be 31” (79cm) wide and 52” (132cm) long or smaller.As a reminder, wagons are not permitted in our parks. Stroller wagons will also no longer be permitted.Loose and dry ice is not permitted in our parks. Reusable ice packs are recommended.Why is smoking no longer allowed at Walt Disney World Resort theme parks, water parks and ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex?, Walt Disney World Resort makes updates from time to time and the removal of smoking areas is intended to provide a more enjoyable experience for everyone who visits.Are electronic cigarettes and vaping permitted at Walt Disney World Resort?, Smoking and vaping are only permitted in designated smoking areas.Where can guests smoke?, Guests may smoke in designated areas located outside the park entry points and in specified areas at Disney Resort hotels and Disney Springs. , Why are you reducing the size of strollers and prohibiting wagons in your theme parks and water parks?, Walt Disney World Resort makes updates from time to time, and the reduction of stroller sizes is intended to ease guest flow and reduce congestion, making the park experience more enjoyable for everyone who visits. Many strollers, including many double jogging strollers, fit within these guidelines.Are stroller-wagons permitted?, Stroller wagons, whether pushed or pulled, will not be permitted at any theme park or water park or at indoor venues at ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex.What if my stroller is larger than the size allowed?, Strollers are available for rent at the parks. Guests who have additional questions on the stroller policy may visit Guest Relations for more information.How do I ensure my stroller falls within the size guidelines?, Strollers should be no larger than 31” (79 cm) wide and 52” (132cm) long when measured across the widest and longest points.Why is loose or dry ice not permitted in your parks?, In order to improve guest flow, ease congestion and streamline the bag-check and entry processes, loose and dry ice is not permitted. Reusable ice packs are recommended.What happens if I need ice for baby food, medicine, or some other item?, Reusable ice packs are recommended. Cups of ice are available at no charge at Food & Beverage locations.Where can guests with disabilities find more information on the rule and policy updates?, Nothing has changed about how we make accommodations for guests with disabilities. Meeting their needs is extremely important to us. Guests with disabilities who have questions or concerns about any of the updates may visit Guest Relations or contact Disability.Services@DisneyParks.com,  or 407-560-2547 to address their needs.
What areas of Walt Disney World Resort permit smoking?
Walt Disney World theme parks, water parks, ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex and Disney resort hotels are smoke-free environments except for designated smoking areas.At Disney Resort hotels, , smoking is permitted in designated outdoor smoking areas. Smoking is not permitted in guest rooms or on balconies. Guests can request location information at the hotel Front Desk.If you have questions about our smoking policy or wish to locate the nearest designated smoking area, please visit our Designated Smoking Areas page,  or ask a Disney Cast Member.Marijuana, Smoking marijuana is not permitted at any time in Disney Resort hotels, even in designated smoking areas.Please Check Our Walt Disney World Resort Rules, We regularly update our Walt Disney World Resort Rules,  to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience. We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort Rules before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions.
Can I smoke on the patio or balcony of my Disney Resort hotel room?
No. Guests may not smoke in their Disney Resort hotel rooms, on patios or on balconies. Each Disney Resort hotel features designated outdoor smoking areas.If you have questions about our smoking policy or wish to locate the nearest designated smoking area, please visit our Designated Smoking Areas page,  or ask a Disney Cast Member.View a complete list of the Disney Resort hotels at Walt Disney World Resort.
How is the Disney Resort hotel smoke-free policy enforced?
To cover the costs of cleaning and restoring the room to a smoke-free condition, a US $250 to US $500 room recovery fee plus tax (based on the Disney Resort hotel and room type) will be charged to Guests who smoke in hotel rooms, on balconies or on patios.Each Disney Resort hotel features designated outdoor smoking areas. The Concierge and Front Desk are available to direct you to the nearest smoking location.View a complete list of the Disney Resort hotels at Walt Disney World Resort.
Is there parking at Disney Springs?
Yes. Self-parking is complimentary in our surface lots and garages. Look for signs directing you to available parking.Valet parking is available in the following 3 areas:Near the entrance to the Orange Garage from 10:00 AM to 2:00 AM, On West Side in front of Cirque du Soleil from 4:00 PM to 2:00 AM, In the Lemon Lot near the World of Disney shop from 10:00 AM to 2:00 AM, The cost of valet parking is $20 and will be collected at the time of pick-up. Gratuity is not included.Designated parking spaces for Guests with disabilities are available in both the Orange and Lime Garages. A valid disability parking permit is required. Wheelchair, ECV,  and stroller rentals,  are available at the nearby Sundries location next to the Town Center bus loop.If you’re staying with us and prefer not to drive, complimentary transportation is available between Disney Resort hotels,  and Disney Springs.Learn more about transportation,  and parking,  at Walt Disney World Resort.
What is Disney Springs? 
Disney Springs is a themed retail, dining and entertainment center inspired by Florida's charming waterfront towns, historic architecture and natural beauty. The sprawling promenade features 4 distinct neighborhoods―The Landing, Marketplace, West Side and Town Center—built around bubbling springs.Learn more about what's happening at Disney Springs on the website, Disney Parks Blog, , or follow @DisneySprings on Twitter for real-time updates.
How much does it cost to park at Disney Springs at Walt Disney World Resort? 
Self-parking in our surface parking lots and parking garages is complimentary...Valet parking is available in the following 3 areas:Near the entrance to the Orange Garage from 10:00 AM to 2:00 AM, On West Side in front of Cirque du Soleil from 4:00 PM to 2:00 AM, In the Lemon Lot near the World of Disney shop from 10:00 AM to 2:00 AM, The cost of valet parking is $20 and will be collected at the time of pick-up. Gratuity is not included.Staying at a Walt Disney World Resort hotel? Take advantage of complimentary transportation by bus or boat. Many area accommodations also provide or arrange transportation to and from Disney Springs.
Is there a way to get to Disney Springs without driving?
If you are staying at a Disney Resort hotel, , we encourage you to use our complimentary bus and water transportation,  to Disney Springs. From Disney's Saratoga Springs Resort & Spa, , a pedestrian bridge lets you walk directly to Disney Springs Marketplace.Bus transportation links Walt Disney World Resort Hotels to a stop at Disney Springs Town Center. These hotels offer water transportation to each of the Disney Springs neighborhoods:Disney's Port Orleans Resort—French Quarter, Disney's Port Orleans Resort—Riverside, Disney's Old Key West Resort, Disney's Saratoga Springs Resort & Spa, Learn more about transportation,  and parking,  at Walt Disney World Resort.
What security measures do you have in place?
We have a comprehensive approach to security that includes measures that are visible and others that are not, including the presence of uniformed police officers. We do not broadly discuss the specifics of our security procedures to avoid compromising their effectiveness.
What types of shopping and dining experiences are at Disney Springs?
From intimate boutiques to stunning flagship locations, Disney Springs is home to over 150 offerings ranging from Disney-themed shops to noteworthy brands. While you're here, be sure you visit the expanded World of Disney,  store, which is the largest Disney character store in the world.There’s so much to see and do at Disney Springs! Stores are brimming with merchandise ranging from fashion apparel and jewelry to collectibles and artwork. Stop for a snack and coffee or cold drink, listen to talented musical performers, or enjoy a gourmet meal at one of the many fine dining restaurants. And cap off your visit with a first-run movie or an exhilarating round of bowling.View the amazing assortment of retail, dining,  and entertainment,  options available at Disney Springs.
Which Walt Disney World golf course do you recommend for beginners?
For beginner and novice golfers, we recommend the shorter and more tranquil experience on Disney's Oak Trail Golf Course.This 9-hole walking course provides a more enjoyable golf experience for beginning golfers and families with smaller children. It is a great place to try to improve your game.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
What will happen if I have to cancel my tee time or reduce the number of players at a Walt Disney World golf course?
If you do not cancel or reduce your number of players 24 hours before your scheduled tee time, you may be subject to a charge on the credit card that you provided when you made your reservation.If your plans or your party size have changed, please call the Golf Master Starter at (407) WDW-GOLF or (407) 939-4653 to cancel or modify your reservation. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. If you made your tee time reservations online, you are also able to cancel online.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Is there a GPS Yardage System on the golf carts at Walt Disney World golf courses?
Yes. A GPS (Global Positioning System) device is located on the golf carts at our 3 championship golf courses. This helpful system provides precise yardages, hole diagrams, pin locations and other useful information. It also helps maintain an enjoyable pace of play for all players.Disney's Oak Trail Golf Course,  is a walking course and GPS systems are not available there.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Is there a cart fee in addition to the stated greens fee for Walt Disney World Resort golf courses?
No. We do not add a cart fee in addition to a player′s greens fee.Our greens fee includes the use of a golf cart (normally shared by 2) equipped with a small cooler, a sand bucket to fill divots, GPS yardage system, front windshields and rear pull-down club covers.Disney′s Oak Trail Golf Course,  is a walking course, and golf carts are not provided or permitted there.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Can you store and transfer my clubs to another Walt Disney World golf course? 
Yes. You are welcome to store your clubs at any Walt Disney World golf course.As of January 1, 2020, a $5 per night per bag storage fee will apply for golf bags that are retained overnight at our facilities before, during and/or after your visit to any Walt Disney World Resort Golf Course. The appropriate charge will be assessed at the time of check-in for your initial round of golf based on how many days you anticipate storing your golf equipment at our facilities.We will also transfer your clubs from one Walt Disney World golf course to another. These transfers are made at the beginning of each day, so please consider this option when planning your schedule.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Are the Walt Disney World Resort golf courses accessible to Guests with disabilities?
Yes. All Walt Disney World Resort golf courses offer single-rider, adaptive golf carts and feature clubhouse accommodations for Guests with disabilities. Please call the Golf Master Starter at (407) WDW-GOLF or (407) 939-4653 for more information or to book your tee time. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Tee time reservations can be made 60 days in advance—or 90 days in advance if you are a Guest of a Disney Resort hotel.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort,  or learn more about how we help accommodate Guests with disabilities at Walt Disney World Resort. 
Do you have locker rooms and shower facilities at the Walt Disney World golf courses?
Yes. We have lockers and shower facilities for men and women at each of our golf courses. Please see the pro shop staff for a locker key. There is no fee for locker usage.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Who operates the Walt Disney World golf courses?
The Walt Disney World golf courses are owned by The Walt Disney Company and operated by Arnold Palmer Golf Management.Arnold Palmer Golf Management is one of the premier golf operators in the world, and we are proud to work with them to provide a world-class golfing experience.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Why is a credit card required with my tee time reservation for a Walt Disney World golf course?
In order to provide you with a better selection of tee times, we require Guests to secure tee time reservations with a credit card. Unfortunately, if a credit card is not required, increased numbers of no-shows take away opportunities for other Guests.Your card will not be charged when the reservation is made. However, you are subject to being charged a cancellation fee of $25 from May to September and $40 from October to April, if you do not cancel your tee time at least 24 hours in advance.If your plans or party size change, please call the Golf Master Starter at (407) WDW-GOLF or (407) 939-4653 to cancel or modify your reservation. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. If you made your tee time reservations online, you are also able to cancel online.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
What is the dress code for the Walt Disney World golf courses?
Men are required to wear slacks or Bermuda-length shorts and collared golf shirts. Denim shorts, jeans, T-shirts, sleeveless shirts, denim shirts and shirts with inappropriate words or images are not permitted.Women are required to wear Bermuda-length shorts, skirts, skorts, capris or slacks. Women may wear sleeveless shirts. Tank-tops or tube-tops are not permitted.Attire that is not appropriate—and which may result in refusal of admittance—includes but is not limited to:Clothing with objectionable material, including obscene language or graphics , Excessively torn clothing , Clothing which, by nature, exposes excessive portions of the skin that may be viewed as inappropriate for a family environment , Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Which Walt Disney World golf course is most appropriate for my skill level? 
Our 3 golf courses are 18-hole championship layouts playing to a par of 72. Each of these courses is suitable for golfers of all skill levels:Disney's Magnolia Golf Course, Disney's Palm Golf Course, Disney's Lake Buena Vista Golf Course, For less-skilled golfers who are still learning to play or families with young children, we recommend our 9-hole walking course, Disney′s Oak Trail Golf Course.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Are there food and beverage carts on the Walt Disney World golf courses?
Yes. We offer food and beverage cart service on our golf courses. Carts offer assorted beverages, snacks, sandwiches and cigars.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
What types of shoes and spikes are permitted on Walt Disney World golf courses?
To preserve the high quality of our greens, we require the use of metal spike alternatives such as soft spikes or spikeless golf shoes on our courses. Tennis shoes and other relatively flat, rubber-soled shoes are also permitted, provided they do not have significant ridges, waffle patterns or a prominent heel.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Is golf club sharing permitted at Walt Disney World golf courses?
Golf club sharing is not permitted. All players are required to have their own bag and clubs.Golf bags are available for rent if you wish to travel with clubs for multiple players in a single bag and split them up when you arrive at the course. We also offer rental clubs and shoes. Golf balls, apparel and accessories are available for purchase at our pro shops.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Will you pair golfers with other players if we do not have a foursome at a championship Walt Disney World golf course?
Yes. In order to give all our Guests the opportunity to play, we do try to pair players into foursomes whenever practical. This practice promotes a consistent pace of play.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
What will happen if I'm late for my tee time at a Walt Disney World golf course?
If you are unavoidably detained and arrive late, our golf staff will do their best to accommodate you whenever possible.However, to provide the best experience for other golfers, we ask that you arrive at least 30 minutes prior to your tee time—to allow for your check-in at the pro shop, golf cart assignment and an adequate warm-up.If your plans or party size have changed, please call the Golf Master Starter at (407) WDW-GOLF or (407) 939-4653 to cancel or modify your reservation. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. If you made your tee time reservation online, you are also able to cancel online.Please try to contact us at least 24 hours before your tee time to cancel or modify your reservation.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
I have a non-player who wants to ride along while I play on a Walt Disney World golf course. Do they have to pay a fee?
Yes. Non-player riders are welcome, but they must pay a nominal fee of $15 USD. The fee covers access to our facilities and golf cart usage.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
We have 5 players. Can we play on a Walt Disney World golf course as a fivesome?
We can accommodate any size party or group of golfers, but we limit players to a maximum of 4 Guests per tee time.A party of 5 would be booked as a threesome and twosome—with the understanding that each of these may be paired to fill out foursomes for each tee time.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Can I bring a cooler with my own beverages to a Walt Disney World golf course?
Personal coolers—or any type of food or beverage storage device—are not permitted on Walt Disney World golf courses.However, each golf cart is equipped with a cooler, and we offer a selection of beverages, snacks and sandwiches for purchase. Outside food and beverage items are not allowed. Comfort stations on the golf courses are equipped with ice machines, cups and water fountains.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Which Walt Disney World golf courses host a PGA TOUR event?
Disney’s Palm Golf Course, Disney’s Magnolia Golf Course,  and Disney's Lake Buena Vista Golf Course,  have all hosted a Disney PGA TOUR tournament. In recent years, Disney’s Palm Golf Course and Disney’s Magnolia Golf Course have hosted a PGA TOUR tournament—with the final 2 rounds played on Disney’s Magnolia Golf Course.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
What happens if I can't finish my round due to rain at a Walt Disney World golf course?
We will provide you with a rain-check to return and complete or restart your round—based on the number of holes that you played.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Are rental clubs and rental shoes available at Walt Disney World golf courses?
Yes. We offer club rentals and shoe rentals. Rental clubs are available for men and women, in both right and left-handed models. Junior clubs are available at Disney's Oak Trail Golf Course, . Rental clubs and shoes do not need to be reserved in advance.We also provide golf tees, so all you need are golf balls and, if necessary, a golf glove. We offer an excellent selection of apparel and accessories at each golf course pro shop.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Is complimentary transportation provided from my Disney Resort hotel to the Walt Disney World Resort golf courses?
Yes. Transportation to and from the golf courses is available with complimentary taxi vouchers from select Walt Disney World Resort hotels.Complimentary transportation is for regular play only. It is not available for group play, group outings or tournaments.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
How long will my round take to play at a Walt Disney World championship golf course? What is the normal pace of play?
Walt Disney World Resort features 3 championship courses:• , Disney's Magnolia Golf Course, • , Disney's Palm Golf Course, • , Disney's Lake Buena Vista Golf Course, All 3 courses are USGA pace-rated between 4 hours and 15 minutes and 4 hours and 35 minutes. We have Player Assistants on the courses at busy times to help monitor the pace, and our GPS system provides pace information to all golfers. Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Why is the tee time that I want not available on a Walt Disney World golf course?
Your ideal tee time request may not be available due to high demand, a group golf event or the routine maintenance needed to keep our courses in excellent condition.The Walt Disney World golf courses are very popular. We recommend that you reserve a tee time,  as far in advance as possible. Tee time reservations can be made 60 days in advance—or 90 days in advance if you are a Guest of a Disney Resort hotel.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
I’m interested in playing a Walt Disney World golf course. Do I need a tee time or can I walk up?
We strongly encourage you to reserve a tee time,  in advance, but we also try to accommodate walk-up golfers.It’s always best to reserve a tee time or call the Golf Master Starter at (407) WDW-GOLF or (407) 939-4653—even if it is just a few hours before you wish to play. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.When staying at a Disney Resort hotel, you can reserve a tee time for 2 or more players up to 90 days in advance of play.In order to provide you with a better selection of tee times, we require Guests to secure tee time reservations with a credit card. Your card will not be charged when the reservation is made. However, you are subject to being charged a cancellation fee of $25 from May to September and $40 from October to April, if you do not cancel your tee time at least 24 hours in advance.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Which Walt Disney World golf courses can I walk?
If you prefer to walk, we recommend playing Disney's Oak Trail Golf Course, . Pull-carts are available for rent at this 9-hole walking course. To provide an enjoyable pace of play, we require players to use golf carts at our 3 championship golf courses:• , Disney's Magnolia Golf Course, • , Disney's Palm Golf Course, • , Disney's Lake Buena Vista Golf Course, The championship golf courses include carts in their greens fee.Learn more about golf at Walt Disney World Resort.
Is complimentary transportation available from Orlando International Airport to my Disney Resort hotel?
Yes. When staying at a Disney Resort hotel, , you may enjoy access to Disney's Magical Express, —a complimentary roundtrip service that whisks you and your luggage between Orlando International Airport and select Disney Resort hotels via a deluxe motorcoach. If you did not select Disney’s Magical Express and include your flight information when you made your reservation, please contact the booking agent for your Disney Resort hotel reservation.
Are car seats permitted on Disney’s Magical Express motorcoaches?
Child safety seats are not recommended for use on the motorcoach. Not all motorcoaches have seat belts and the seat belts that may be present may not properly secure the child safety seat.Children can sit on an adult's lap or occupy their own seat. Child safety seats may be stowed in the storage compartment underneath the motorcoach.
What are the nearest airports to the Walt Disney World Resort?
Your best option is to fly into Orlando International Airport (MCO). From there, Disney Resort hotel,  Guests can take Disney’s Magical Express service, a complimentary roundtrip service that whisks you between Orlando International Airport and your Disney Resort hotel via a deluxe motorcoach. Orlando Sanford International Airport (SFB) is another option, but Disney’s Magical Express service is not available at this location.Disney’s Magical Express service will no longer provide luggage delivery for those arriving to and departing from the airport. Resort Airline Check-In Service is also no longer available.Make a Disney’s Magical Express Service Reservation, To make a reservation, select Disney’s Magical Express service when you make your online vacation reservation and include your flight information, or contact the booking agent for your Disney Resort hotel reservation.How to Handle Your Luggage on Your Trip, Guests who choose to use Disney’s Magical Express service will be responsible for picking up any of their checked luggage from the airport’s baggage claim area, so that it can be loaded onto the motorcoach to their Disney Resort hotel. Please know that your luggage will travel with you to your Disney Resort hotel.Luggage assistance will be available at the front of your Disney Resort hotel, including luggage storage and/or transport to the room.Upon your departure, please ensure your luggage is with you and is loaded onto the motorcoach so you can check it in with your airline once you reach the airport.Locate Disney’s Magical Express Service, Disney’s Magical Express service is located at the Main Terminal Building in Terminal B, Level 1 in the Ground Transportation area.Domestic Arrivals, Take the train from your arrival gate to the Main Terminal, disembarking on Level 3. You will need to claim your luggage on Level 2 before proceeding to Disney’s Magical Express service, located in the Ground Transportation Area in Terminal B, Level 1.Guests claiming their luggage in Terminal A of the airport must return to Level 3 to cross to Terminal B before continuing to Level 1. Upon arrival at Disney's Magical Express welcome center, please let us know if you will need assistance boarding the motorcoach.International Arrivals, Upon exiting your aircraft, enter the U.S. Immigration checkpoint. After retrieving your luggage, proceed to the Customs checkpoint. When exiting the Customs area, keep your checked bags with you to travel on the motorcoach.Take the train to the Main Terminal Building where you will arrive on Level 3. Disney's Magical Express service is located in Terminal B, Level 1. Guests arriving in Terminal A of the airport are advised to cross to Terminal B before proceeding down to Level 1. Upon arrival at Disney’s Magical Express welcome center, please let us know if you will need assistance boarding the motorcoach.Learn more about Disney’s Magical Express.

On the day I depart from my Disney Resort hotel for Orlando International Airport, how will I know what time a Disney's Magical Express motorcoach will pick me up?
The day before you check out, you’ll receive a transportation notice advising you of the motorcoach departure time, which will be approximately 3 hours prior to your scheduled departure time for domestic flights and 4 hours prior to your scheduled departure time for international flights. You are responsible for bringing your luggage to the motorcoach departure location.If you do not receive this information, please speak to your Disney Resort hotel Concierge or call (866) 599-0951. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. , Be sure to have your Transportation Notice on hand when it’s time for your Disney’s Magical Express departure. Your motorcoach driver will collect the Transportation Notice prior to boarding. Please note: MagicBands cannot be used to check in for your trip from your Disney Resort hotel to Orlando International Airport.Learn more about Disney’s Magical Express.

Are Disney Transportation options available for service animals and pets at Walt Disney World Resort?
Select Disney transportation options are available for Guests traveling with service animals and pets at Walt Disney World Resort.Service Animals, Service animals may accompany their owners on Disney Transportation motorcoaches, monorails and watercraft.Pets, Pet dogs may accompany their owners on internal buses at Disney’s Fort Wilderness Resort & Campground,  and Disney’s Port Orleans Resort, . No other pets are permitted on these buses.Only service animals are allowed on Disney Transportation motorcoaches, monorails or watercraft.
Are service animals and pets permitted on Disney’s Magical Express motorcoaches?
Disney’s Magical Express is available for Guests traveling with service animals and pets at Walt Disney World Resort.Service Animals, Service animals may travel on the Disney’s Magical Express motorcoach in the passenger cabin with their owners.Pets, Pet dogs may travel to a dog-friendly resort on the Disney’s Magical Express motorcoach in the passenger cabin while in a pet carrier. The pet carrier must be provided by the owner, and it must be able to fit safely in a seat on the motorcoach.No other pets are permitted in the passenger cabin or the storage compartment.Learn more about Disney’s Magical Express,  or accommodations for Guests with disabilities at Walt Disney World Resort.

I am an Annual Passholder with a MagicBand and I have a reservation at a Disney Resort hotel. Can I get another MagicBand?
You are eligible to receive a new MagicBand,  by staying at a Disney Resort hotel with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 or purchasing one or you can customize and order a new MagicBand.If you like your current MagicBand, you can continue to use it along with your new MagicBand.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.Getting multiple MagicBands or cards does not give you multiple entitlements, such as park admission. Also, once a MagicBand or card is linked to a person, it cannot be transferred to another person. , If you have multiple MagicBands or cards, you can manage which MagicBands and Cards are active in My Profile, . Don’t see your MagicBand? You may need to link your Resort hotel reservation, link your Annual Pass,  or link the MagicBand,  to your Disney account.
When does my Walt Disney World Annual Pass expire?
If you have linked your Annual Pass to your Disney account, , you can check the expiration date on the My Reservations,  or My Profile,  pages of My Disney Experience, . Please note that the Water Park After 2 Annual Pass will only appear in My Reservations.We can also provide your Annual Pass expiration date at any Walt Disney World theme park ticket window or a Disney Springs , Guest Relations,  location. To verify your identity, please bring a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.
Why don’t I see my Theme Park Annual Pass in the My Reservations or My Profile sections of My Disney Experience?
We apologize that your pass is not showing up. Even if you have previously added your annual pass to disneyworld.com, you may need to link it again to ensure that it is connected to My Disney Experience.Link your annual pass to My Disney Experience.If you linked your annual pass within the last 48 hours, please wait until 48 hours have passed and check again. If you still do not see your annual pass after 48 hours, please double-check that the pass has not already expired. Fortunately, you can renew your annual pass online.If you have tried to link your annual pass and confirmed that it has not expired, contact us,  and we will help.Water Park Annual Passes only appear in the My Reservations,  section of My Disney Experience, not on the About Me,  page in the My Profile,  section.The linking process requires that you have your annual pass in your possession, as you will need the ID numbers printed on the pass. You will also need to sign into your Disney account.Learn more about annual passes for Walt Disney World Resort.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.
How do I renew my Annual Pass?
There are 3 convenient ways to renew your Annual Pass:Renew online, Renew at any Walt Disney World Resort theme park ticket window or Disney Springs Guest Relations location.Renew over the phone by calling (407) 560-PASS or (407) 560-7277. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.If you are renewing through the Monthly Payment Program for Florida residents, phone renewals are not available. However, you can renew online, in person at a theme park ticket window or Guest Relations location. Annual Passes can be renewed up to 60 days before and 30 days after expiration.Though the Annual Pass owner does not need to be present for renewal, each Annual Pass owner will need to be present at the ticket window to receive his or her pass.Learn more about Annual Passes,  or purchase a new Annual Pass.

I’m an Annual Passholder who opted to cancel my annual pass, and I may be eligible for a refund. How will annual pass refunds be calculated?
If you elected to cancel your pass(es), here’s how your refund will be calculated:Partial Refund Eligibility/Calculation, The refund amount, if any, for each pass circumstance is unique and based on factors such as: new or renewal, down payment amount, refunds to date, activation date, etc.If the total amount that you paid for your pass(es) (minus any refunds already given and any payments waived, returned or not collected) exceeds the “usable value” (see below) of your pass(es), that excess will be refunded to you.The usable value of your pass(es) equals the total sale price of your pass(es) multiplied by the number of days that you could have visited any park prior to March 16 and divided by the total number of access days to any park permitted under the pass(es) at pass activation.If you made a payment between July 11, 2020 and August 11, 2020 or a payment between March 14, 2020 and April 4, 2020 that was not already refunded, your refund will be at least the amount of any such payment(s).How to Take Action, If you have already elected to cancel your pass(es), this will be automatically processed for your pass(es). You do not need to take any additional action.If you have not selected any option (no action) and would like to select this option to cancel your pass(es), please refer to the email from Disney Destinations on July 14, 2020 and use the personalized link available through August 11, 2020. Or, you may call V.I.PASSHOLDER Support at (407) 939-7277. We appreciate your patience as we answer all inquiries.If you previously took action to elect to continue with your pass(es) and now would like to cancel your pass(es), please call V.I.PASSHOLDER Support at (407) 939-7277. If you have further questions, concerns or unique circumstances, now or after August 11, please contact V.I.PASSHOLDER Support for assistance. We appreciate your patience as we answer all inquiries.
I am an Annual Passholder with a MagicBand and an annual pass card. What should I bring to the Walt Disney World theme parks?
Please bring your MagicBand, , annual pass card and a valid photo ID—such as a driver’s license or passport.Your MagicBand can be used for theme park admission.Your annual pass card enables you to access your Passholder entitlements—including theme park admission, food and merchandise discounts and complimentary standard theme park parking, if your pass includes parking. The pass card must be presented—along with a photo ID—at the time of purchase, when you book and when you redeem any Passholder offer.Learn more about annual passes,  or purchase a new pass.
I am a member of Club 33 at Disneyland Park in California and I am visiting Walt Disney World Resort in Florida. How do I receive my Club 33 dining and merchandise discounts?
Please bring your Club 33 Membership Card with you to Walt Disney World Resort to use for theme park admission and to access your Club 33 dining and merchandise discounts. To verify your identity, please bring a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.If both your MagicBand and Club 33 Membership Card are linked to your Disney account, , you can use your MagicBand for entry at Walt Disney World theme parks, but you will still need your Club 33 Membership Card to receive your member discounts.If you have any questions or you need help, please call Club 33 Member Services at (714) 300-7747. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
I am a member of Club 33 at Disneyland Park in California, and I am visiting Walt Disney World Resort in Florida. Do I receive a MagicBand?
If you are a member of Club 33, you are eligible to receive a MagicBand.Please follow these simple steps at least 11 days before you plan to visit Walt Disney World Resort and your MagicBand will be delivered straight to your home:Create,  or sign into,  your Disney account.Link your Club 33 Membership Card to your Disney account, , if you have not already done so. Customize your MagicBand.Please continue to bring your Club 33 Membership Card to both the Disneyland Resort and Walt Disney World Resort. You will need the Club 33 Membership Card for admission to Disneyland Resort theme parks and for your Club 33 discounts at both the Disneyland Resort and Walt Disney World Resort. To verify your identity, please bring a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport. MagicBand orders cannot be shipped to all countries.If you have any questions or you need help, please call Club 33 Member Services at (714) 300-7747. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
I’m an Annual Passholder who opted to continue my annual pass, and I may be eligible for a refund due to the parks closure. How will annual pass refunds be calculated?
If you previously elected to have payments waived (not postponed) during the park closure period, you may be eligible to receive a refund. No additional action is required.Partial Refund Eligibility/Calculation, The refund amount, if any, for each pass circumstance is unique and based on factors such as: new or renewal, down payment amount, refunds to date, future payments, etc.If the total amount that you already paid for your pass(es) (minus any refunds already given and any payments waived, returned or not collected) plus the total amount that you are obligated to pay for your pass(es) in future payments that are not yet due exceeds the “usable value” (see below) of your pass(es), that excess will be automatically refunded to you.The usable value of your pass(es) equals the total sale price of your pass(es) multiplied by the total number of access days to any park permitted under the pass(es) at pass activation excluding the period March 16 – July 10 (March 16 – July 14 if your pass(es) only allow admission to Epcot) and divided by the total number of access days to any park permitted under the pass(es) at pass activation.
I have an annual pass that includes Disney PhotoPass downloads. How do I use Disney PhotoPass Service?
It’s easy to get started! If your pass,  includes Disney PhotoPass downloads, all you need to do is link your valid annual pass to your Disney account,  and you’re ready to visit the Walt Disney World theme parks and begin enjoying Disney PhotoPass Service.While at Walt Disney World Resort, you may use your annual pass, MagicBand,  or Disney PhotoPass card to link photos to your Disney account—including attraction and dining photos.You can view and download eligible photos linked to your Disney account on the Photos & Videos page,  or with the My Disney Experience mobile app, . If you’re not seeing your photos on the Photos & Videos page, please double check that you have linked all relevant annual passes, MagicBands and Disney PhotoPass cards to your Disney account.Have you linked your pass and still need help downloading your photos? View detailed instructions on how to download photos.Learn more about Walt Disney World annual passes—including details on which passes include Disney PhotoPass downloads.

I am a Walt Disney World Annual Passholder. How far in advance can I make FastPass+ selections?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.Annual Passholders may secure up to 3 experiences per day up to 30 days in advance. Your pass allows you to plan 7 days of FastPass+ selections,  within any 30-day period for one park per day. Secure up to 3 experiences per day up to 30 days in advance—starting at 7:00 AM Eastern Time. And if plans change, it’s easy to update or cancel your selections.Passholders with reservations at a Disney Resort hotel,  can start making FastPass+ selections up to 60 days prior to check-in for the entire length of your stay. Please note that if your length of stay is longer than 2 weeks, FastPass+ selections can be made for up to 14 days.If you have a valid Walt Disney World Annual Pass, please follow these simple steps:Create,  or sign into,  your Disney account.Link your Annual Pass or Passes to your,  account, if you have not already done so.Make your FastPass+ selections.As with Guests using tickets, once you redeem your initial set of FastPass+ selections (or the last arrival window has passed), you can make another FastPass+ selection for the same day at an in-park kiosk,  or using your mobile device. After you redeem your initial 3 selections, use the app or head to a kiosk to make another selection. If your Annual Pass permits you to visit a second park on the same day, you have the option to make additional FastPass+ selections at another park—even if you’re in a different park from your original selections!, For a greater range of choices, we recommend you make FastPass+ selections,  early. If you prefer to be spontaneous, all attractions and Character Greetings provide standby entrances so you can decide as you go.If you have not yet received a MagicBand, , you’ll need to link your Annual Pass to your Disney account,  and customize your MagicBand,  at least 11 days before you plan to visit Walt Disney World Resort. Your MagicBand will be shipped to your home (shipping available to U.S. addresses only).For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.Valid theme park admission required. FastPass+ attractions and entertainment experiences, the number of selections you can make and available arrival windows are limited. Certain MyMagic+ features and benefits require online registration.
I am an Annual Passholder and I don’t want to use a MagicBand. Can I still use FastPass+ service?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. MagicBands,  are a convenient option for making your Walt Disney World visit more fun and carefree than ever, but if you prefer not to use a MagicBand, you can continue to use your annual pass for park admission, FastPass+,  service and Passholder discounts.If you are purchasing a new pass, you can receive your pass at any theme park or Disney Springs ticket sales location. What proof of residence will I need to provide in order to purchase a Florida Resident park ticket or annual pass?
You’ll need to provide proof of a Florida residential address in order to purchase a Florida Resident park ticket or annual pass. For each ticket or pass purchased for an adult, you may provide any of the following:Valid Florida driver’s license (must have a Florida address), Valid Florida state-issued ID card (must have a Florida address), Valid Florida-based military ID, *For your convenience, Florida residents with any of the above listed identification can now verify their residency online, which means you can bypass Guest Relations and go straight to the parks! Simply fill out the “Your Florida Resident Information” form upon check-out when you purchase tickets through Disneyworld.com or complete the “Customize Your Tickets” step when you purchase through the My Disney Experience app.If you do not have one of the IDs indicated above, then you must provide one of the following—dated within the past 2 months—evidencing a Florida residential address, along with a corresponding picture ID (passport, driver's license, state identification card):Proof of Current Mortgage, You may use a monthly mortgage statement from within the past 2 months; it may not be more than 2 months old. Deeds, mortgage contracts, mortgage payment booklets and leases are not accepted.Bills, Policies or Registration, Current homeowner's insurance policy or bill, Current automobile registration, insurance policy or bill, Current Utility bill (power / phone / cable / water), Bills can be no more than 2 months old (P.O. Boxes are not accepted as proof of residency), Mail, Mail from financial institutions, including checking, savings or investment account statements, Mail from federal, state, county or city government agencies, Mail can be no more than 2 months old (P.O. Boxes are not accepted as proof of residency), Additional members of the same household must only provide proof of same residential address.Current statements and bills printed from electronic versions are accepted, along with electronic bills provided via smart phones and tablet devices.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.
How do I give someone theme park tickets as a gift?
It’s easy to give Walt Disney World theme park tickets as a gift. Select the tickets that you wish to give,  and proceed to checkout.In the “Guest Information” section on the Checkout page, select the “This order will be a gift” checkbox. Enter the first and last name of the Guest and make your purchase.Please keep in mind that gift orders will not be available immediately. It may take up to 24 hours after you received your email order confirmation before the recipient can pick up their tickets.Picking Up Gift Tickets, To pick up the ticket order at the park Main Entrance ticket window:The gift recipient will need to present the gift receipt and a valid government-issued photo ID.The name you provided for the gift recipient must match the name on the ID. If the recipient is a minor, the minor's parent or legal guardian will need to accompany the minor and present a valid government-issued photo ID.Ready to give some magic? Select your tickets!
How do I renew someone else's annual pass as a gift?
To renew an existing annual pass as a gift, please call (407) 560-7277. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. After you pay in full, we will mail you a renewal certificate, which you can give to the gift recipient. The recipient can take the renewal certificate to a park Main Entrance ticket window to complete their annual pass renewal.If you’d prefer to renew in person, please visit a park Main Entrance ticket window along with the Annual Passholder. You must both be present to complete the renewal of the pass.Learn more about annual passes.
I linked an Annual Pass to the wrong person in My Disney Experience. How can I match the Annual Pass to the correct person?
If an Annual Pass has not yet been used to enter a park, you can match it online to the correct person in the My Reservations,  section of My Disney Experience.On the My Reservations page, locate the pass that you wish to reassign in the “Paperless Tickets” section and select the “Reassign Ticket” link associated with the pass. You will then be able to match the Annual Pass to the correct person on your Family & Friends list.If you cannot find the Annual Pass that you wish to reassign, please make sure that “Show All” is selected in the dropdown menu in the top-left corner and “My Family” is selected in the dropdown menu in the top-right corner. If you still do not see the Annual Pass, double-check that the person to which the pass is linked is still connected to your Family & Friends list,  and that you are sharing information,  with that person.If an Annual Pass has been used to enter a park, you are unable to reassign it online. Please visit the Guest Relations location at the Main Entrance of any Walt Disney World theme park for assistance.Learn more about Annual Passes for Walt Disney World Resort.
I received an email that asked me to link my Annual Pass to My Disney Experience. How do I link my Annual Pass?
Link your Annual Pass with My Disney Experience, . Once your Theme Park Annual Pass is linked, you will see it listed on the About Me,  page in the My Profile,  section and the My Reservations,  section. You can also add additional Annual Passes for yourself or people on your Family & Friends,  list by selecting the “Add Another Walt Disney World Pass” link on the About Me page.Water Park Annual Passes only appear in the My Reservations,  section of My Disney Experience, not on the About Me,  page in the My Profile,  section.The linking process requires that you have your Annual Pass in your possession, as you will need the ID numbers printed on the pass. You will also need to sign into your Disney account.Learn more about Annual Passes for Walt Disney World Resort.
Can I link Annual Passes to My Disney Experience for my family and friends? 
Yes! You can link Annual Passes to family and friends if they are connected to your  Family & Friends list. Link an Annual Pass to My Disney Experience.After you have entered the Annual Pass ID numbers (printed on the pass), you will be asked to match each pass with a person on your Family & Friends list. It’s that easy! If there are several Annual Passes that you wish to link, you are able to add multiple passes at the same time.Learn more about Annual Passes for Walt Disney World Resort.
I recently purchased an annual pass on disneyworld.com and have an exchange certificate. How do I customize and order my MagicBand?

I’m an Annual Passholder. How often will I receive the Mickey Monitor newsletter?
The Mickey Monitor newsletter is mailed out every February, May, August and November, and each edition includes additional benefits and program updates.  Remember: only one newsletter will be sent per active Walt Disney World Passholder household, and is exclusively available in the United States and Puerto Rico.
What is the best way to make or modify my FastPass+ selections when I am visiting a Walt Disney World theme park?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.There are 3 different ways you can make, update or cancel FastPass+ selections while you’re at any of the theme parks:Open the My Disney Experience app,  on your mobile device and tap FastPass+ in the main menu (linked theme park admission required), Use the browser on your mobile device to go to disneyworld.com and sign in, then navigate to the FastPass+ page,  (linked park admission required), Use one of the in-park FastPass+ kiosks, Once you redeem your initial set of FastPass+ selections (or the last arrival window has passed), you can make another FastPass+ selection for the same day at an in-park kiosk,  or using your mobile device, based on availability. After you redeem the additional FastPass+ pick, you can make more selections (one at a time) up to park closing.If you have questions about FastPass+ service or your MagicBand, please stop by any Guest Relations,  location and we’ll be happy to help you.For a greater range of choices, we recommend you make FastPass+ selections early. If you prefer to be spontaneous, all attractions and Character Greetings provide standby entrances so you can decide as you go.Valid theme park admission required. FastPass+ attractions and entertainment experiences, the number of selections you can make and available arrival windows are limited. Certain MyMagic+ features and benefits require online registration.
Can I have multiple active MagicBands or cards?
Yes. If you have multiple MagicBands,  or cards linked to your Disney account, you can continue to use as many as your wrists and pockets can carry.However, getting multiple MagicBands or cards does not give you multiple entitlements, such as additional park admission. Also, once a MagicBand or card is linked to a person, it cannot be transferred to another person.You have the ability to manage which MagicBands and cards are active in My Profile, . Don’t see your MagicBand? You may need to link your Resort hotel reservation, link your Annual Pass,  or link the MagicBand,  to your Disney account.

Can I make FastPass+ selections for more than one theme park in a single day? 
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.After you use your initial FastPass+ selections at the first park you visit, use a FastPass+ kiosk,  in the second park to make additional FastPass+ selections (one at a time) at a kiosk or using the mobile app at the second park you visit that day, up to park closing.When you also book a stay at a Walt Disney World Resort hotel, , you can start making your FastPass+ selections as early as 60 days―plus the number of days of your stay―prior to your check-in date.For a greater range of choices, we recommend you make FastPass+ selections early. If you prefer to be spontaneous, all attractions and Character Greetings provide standby entrances so you can decide as you go.Valid theme park admission required. FastPass+ attractions and entertainment experiences, the number of selections you can make and available arrival windows are limited. Certain MyMagic+ features and benefits require online registration.Link theme park admission to your Disney account,  or make FastPass+ selections.
I’m an Annual Passholder who has paid in full. I opted to cancel my annual pass and I may be eligible for a refund. How will annual pass refunds be calculated?
If you elected to cancel your pass(es), here’s how your refund will be calculated:Partial Refund Eligibility/Calculation, The refund amount, if any, for each pass is unique and based on factors such as: new or renewal, refunds to date, and activation date.If the total amount that you paid for your pass(es) (minus any refunds already given) exceeds the “usable value” (see below) of your pass(es), that excess will be refunded to you.The usable value of your pass(es) equals the total sale price of your pass(es) multiplied by the number of days that you could have visited any park prior to March 16 and divided by the total number of access days to any park permitted under the pass(es) at pass activation.How to Take Action, If you have already elected to cancel your pass(es), this will be automatically processed for your pass(es). You do not need to take any additional action.If you have not selected any option (no action) and would like to cancel your pass(es), please refer to the email from Disney Destinations on July 14, 2020 and use the personalized link available through August 11, 2020. Or, you may contact V.I.PASSHOLDER Support at (407) 939-7277. If you have further questions, concerns or unique circumstances, now or after August 11, please contact V.I.PASSHOLDER Support for assistance. We appreciate your patience as we answer all inquiries.If you previously took action to elect to continue with your pass(es) and now would like to cancel your pass(es), please call V.I.PASSHOLDER Support at (407) 939-7277. We appreciate your patience as we answer all inquiries.
I am an Annual Passholder. Can I pick up my MagicBand the next time I visit Walt Disney World Resort?
Unfortunately, we are not able to provide Passholders with their MagicBands when they arrive at Walt Disney World Resort. However, getting your new MagicBand is easy! Just follow these simple steps:Create,  or sign into,  your Disney account.Link your annual pass or passes to your Disney account, . Your pass may have been linked automatically when you purchased it on disneyworld.com.Activate your pass at any Walt Disney World theme park ticket window or Disney Springs Guest Relations,  location. Please bring your exchange certificate and a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.Use your annual pass to enter a Walt Disney World theme park or water park.Customize your MagicBand.Once you have completed steps 1 through 5, your MagicBand will be delivered directly to your home. If you would like to use your MagicBand during your next Walt Disney World vacation, please be sure to complete these steps at least 11 days prior to your visit.If it is within 11 days of your next theme park visit or your MagicBand did not arrive as scheduled, you can still enjoy the Walt Disney World theme parks. Your Passholder card—with a photo ID—remains valid for theme park entry until it expires. You can use your new MagicBand when you come back the next time!, MagicBand orders cannot be shipped to all countries.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.

Yes. What proof of residence will I need to provide in order to purchase a Florida Resident park ticket or annual pass?
You’ll need to provide proof of a Florida residential address in order to purchase a Florida Resident park ticket or annual pass. For each ticket or pass purchased for an adult, you may provide any of the following:Valid Florida driver’s license (must have a Florida address), Valid Florida state-issued ID card (must have a Florida address), Valid Florida-based military ID, *For your convenience, Florida residents with any of the above listed identification can now verify their residency online, which means you can bypass Guest Relations and go straight to the parks! Simply fill out the “Your Florida Resident Information” form upon check-out when you purchase tickets through Disneyworld.com or complete the “Customize Your Tickets” step when you purchase through the My Disney Experience app.If you do not have one of the IDs indicated above, then you must provide one of the following—dated within the past 2 months—evidencing a Florida residential address, along with a corresponding picture ID (passport, driver's license, state identification card):Proof of Current Mortgage, You may use a monthly mortgage statement from within the past 2 months; it may not be more than 2 months old. Deeds, mortgage contracts, mortgage payment booklets and leases are not accepted.Bills, Policies or Registration, Current homeowner's insurance policy or bill, Current automobile registration, insurance policy or bill, Current Utility bill (power / phone / cable / water), Bills can be no more than 2 months old (P.O. Boxes are not accepted as proof of residency), Mail, Mail from financial institutions, including checking, savings or investment account statements, Mail from federal, state, county or city government agencies, Mail can be no more than 2 months old (P.O. Boxes are not accepted as proof of residency), Additional members of the same household must only provide proof of same residential address.Current statements and bills printed from electronic versions are accepted, along with electronic bills provided via smart phones and tablet devices.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.

When can I renew my Annual Pass?
You can renew your Annual Pass up to 60 days before and 30 days after the pass expiration date. Keep in mind that your renewed Annual Pass will expire one year from your Anniversary Date, regardless of when you actually renew.There are 3 convenient ways to renew:Renew online, Renew at any Walt Disney World Resort theme park ticket window or Disney Springs Guest Relations location.Renew over the phone by calling (407) 560-PASS or (407) 560-7277. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.If you are renewing through the Monthly Payment Program for Florida residents, phone renewals are not available. However, you can renew online, in person at a theme park ticket window or Guest Relations location.Though the Annual Pass owner does not need to be present for renewal, each Annual Pass owner will need to be present at the ticket window to receive his or her pass.Learn more about Annual Passes,  or purchase a new Annual Pass.
How do I access FastPass+ service using my Annual Pass?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.If you have a valid Walt Disney World Annual Pass, please follow these simple steps to make your FastPass+ selections:Create,  or sign into,  your Disney account.Link your Annual Pass or Passes,  to your account, if you have not already done so.Access FastPass+ service.Annual Passholders can make FastPass+ selections up to 30 days in advance. Secure up to 3 FastPass+ selections for one park per day, for up to 7 days. If plans change, it’s easy to update or cancel your selections, , subject to availability.Passholders with reservations at a Walt Disney World Resort hotel,  can start making FastPass+ selections as early as 60 days prior to the check-in date―and can secure FastPass+ selections for the length of stay or up to 7 days. Please note that if your length of stay is longer than two weeks, FastPass+ selections can be made for up to 14 days.Once you redeem your initial set of FastPass+ selections (or the last arrival window has passed), you can make another FastPass+ selection for the same day at an in-park kiosk,  or on your mobile device. After you redeem the additional FastPass+ pick, you can make more selections (one at a time) up to park closing.If your Annual Pass permits you to visit a second park on the same day, after you use your initial FastPass+ selections at the first park you visit, you have the option to make additional FastPass+ selections at an in-park kiosk or using your mobile device in the second park.For a greater range of choices, we recommend you make FastPass+ selections early, . If you prefer to be spontaneous, all attractions and Character Greetings provide standby entrances so you can decide as you go.Valid theme park admission required. FastPass+ attractions and entertainment experiences, the number of selections you can make and available arrival windows are limited. Certain MyMagic+ features and benefits require online registration.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.

What is the difference between the Florida Resident Disney Silver Pass and the Florida Resident Theme Park Select Pass?
The Florida Resident Disney Silver Pass is designed for Guests who prefer access to all 4 parks and are flexible with the time of year they visit.The Florida Resident Theme Park Select Pass is designed for Guests who prefer more overall daily access to Walt Disney World Resort throughout the year—and are flexible with the park they have access to when they visit. Additional highlights of the Florida Resident Theme Park Select Pass include:Admission during certain times of the year to select theme parks (, blockout dates apply,  and vary by park), 325 days or more of admission to at least one theme park—that’s more days annually when compared to the Disney Silver Pass, Existing blockout dates for the pass may be lifted from time to time, Learn more about annual pass blockout dates, For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.

What is the Florida Resident Theme Park Select Pass?
The Florida Resident Theme Park Select Pass is ideal for Florida residents who are looking for access to at least one theme park during most times of the year. This pass includes 325 days or more of admission to at least one theme park. That’s more days annually when compared to the Disney Silver Pass.The Florida Resident Theme Park Select Pass is $439—or just $28 per month after down payment.Learn more about annual pass blockout dates, For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.

Can I view Annual Passes that are linked to other people in My Disney Experience?
In the My Reservations,  section of My Disney Experience, , you are able to view Annual Passes linked to people connected to your Family & Friends list,  if you are sharing information,  with that person. Look for Annual Passes in the “Paperless Tickets” section of My Reservations.If you cannot find the Annual Pass that you wish to reassign, please make sure that “Show All” is selected in the dropdown menu in the top-left corner and “My Family” is selected in the dropdown menu in the top-right corner. If you still do not see the Annual Pass, double-check that the person to which the pass is linked is still connected to your Family & Friends,  list and that you are sharing information,  with that person.Learn more about Annual Passes for Walt Disney World Resort.
I am an Annual Passholder at Walt Disney World Resort. How do I receive Annual Passholder discounts and benefits on disneyworld.com?

I have a Water Park After 2 Annual Pass. Do I receive a MagicBand?
No. Having a Water Park After 2 Annual Pass does not make you eligible to receive a MagicBand.However, if you already have a MagicBand—perhaps through a reservation at a Disney Resort hotel, —and both the MagicBand and unexpired Annual Pass are linked to your Disney account, , you are able to use the MagicBand to access the admission benefits of your Annual Pass to enter the Disney Water Parks.If you have not already received a new RF-enabled Water Park After 2 Annual Pass, you may need to exchange your older pass for a new card at the Disney’s Typhoon Lagoon Water Park,  or Disney’s Blizzard Beach Water Park,  ticket window.
I’m a Platinum Plus or Premier Annual Passholder. How will the partial refund for lost water park access be calculated?
If you are a Platinum Plus or Premier Annual Passholder with a valid pass, here’s how your refund will be calculated:The refund amount, if any, for each pass is unique and based on factors such as: new or renewal, refunds to date, and activation date.If you are a Platinum Plus Passholder, this partial refund amount is based on the price you paid for your Platinum Plus pass compared to the price of a Platinum Annual Pass at the time of your purchase prorated by the number of days left on your pass from 7/11/2020 - 3/6/2021. New Platinum Plus Passholders will receive $0.27 per day, Platinum Plus Passholders who renewed will receive $0.23 per day, If you are a Premier Passholder, you will receive a pro-rated refund based on the difference between a Walt Disney World Platinum Plus pass with water park access, compared to the price of a Platinum pass, pro-rated by the number of days left on your pass from 7/11/2020 - 3/6/2021, . (Excluding any additional extensions you may be eligible for due to to the continued closure of Disneyland Resort, .), This partial refund will be automatically processed for your pass(es). You do not need to take any additional action.If you have further questions, concerns or unique circumstances, please contact V.I.PASSHOLDER Support for assistance. We appreciate your patience as we answer all inquiries.
Why does the pro-rated refund for lost water park access begin on 7/11/2020?
During the Walt Disney World closure, Annual Passholders had the option of a partial refund or an extension of their pass.Passholders that chose a partial refund during the initial closure period 3/16/2020 - 7/10/2020 have already received a partial refund. The remaining refund is based on number of days remaining on the pass prior to Water Park reopening.Passholders that chose to extend their pass will receive a refund for Water Park access lost based on the extended number of days remaining on their pass from 7/11/2020 – 3/6/2021.
Can I order my food using the My Disney Experience app?
Yes—you can use Mobile Food and Beverage Ordering on the My Disney Experience app,  at select quick-service restaurants.Mobile Food and Beverage Ordering, You can avoid the line to order and pay at select quick-service restaurants by using the My Disney Experience app on your mobile device. Guests can also use their Disney dining plan,  to make a mobile order purchase. Learn more about Mobile Food and Beverage Ordering—including a list of participating locations.
