Which Walt Disney World restaurants take reservations?
Select restaurants at our 4 theme parks, Disney Resort hotels and Disney Springs take reservations. In addition, select dinner shows and special dining events also take reservations. Book reservations online!,  Please note, lounges and quick-service restaurants do not offer reservations.View a complete list of locations that take dining reservations.Disney Dining Plans, Disney dining plans,  are a convenient and flexible way to enjoy many of the restaurants and food-service locations at Walt Disney World Resort. When planning your vacation, consider purchasing a Disney Resort Hotel Package,  with a dining plan—which includes a Disney Resort hotel stay and theme park tickets.Learn more about vacation packages with Disney dining plans.Other Important Details, Reservation availability for select Walt Disney World restaurants typically begins each day at approximately 5:45 AM.Please be aware that if you cancel a restaurant reservation, your previously scheduled reservation time will immediately be made available to another Guest.All newly introduced dining events—such as special dining experiences and dessert parties—can typically be booked beginning at 7:00 AM on the day their offers become available.
When can I make advance reservations for experiences at Walt Disney World Resort, such as dining reservations and available Enchanting Extras Collection experiences?
All Guests may now make advance reservations for dining and other experiences up to 60 days in advance. In addition, Disney Resort hotel Guests can make reservations up to 60 days in advance plus the length of their stay (up to 10 days).Dining reservations can be booked online, Enchanting Extras Collection experiences can be booked by calling (407) 939-6690—or (800) 800-9800 for Disney Vacation Club Members, Here are some additional details to help you plan:In-Park Dining, With the opening of Magic Kingdom park and Disney’s Animal Kingdom theme park on July 11, followed by EPCOT and Disney’s Hollywood Studios on July 15, Guests will need valid park admission and a reservation for park entry,  through the new Disney Park Pass system—as well as a dining reservation—to dine at in-park, table-service restaurants. Dining reservations do not guarantee admission to the park.Disney Resort Hotel Dining, Planning to dine at a table-service restaurant in a Disney Resort hotel? A confirmed dining reservation is required for day Guests (those not staying overnight) and is highly recommended for Guests staying overnight at a Disney Resort hotel.Disney Springs Dining, Select dining locations at Disney Springs,  are currently accepting reservations. Check availability and make reservations online now.Other Important Information, In order to foster physical distancing during this time, upon reopening, our offerings, restaurants and other experiences such as behind-the-scenes tours will be limited in capacity, while other experiences may remain closed.
How do I make arrangements for Disney Character Dining?
The theme parks and Disney Resort hotels at Walt Disney World Resort offer a variety of Character Dining opportunities. See all Character Dining venues.Character Dining is very popular, and we strongly recommend that you make reservations,  in advance.
Why is a credit card required to make a dining reservation?
We require your credit card to make a dining reservation and use it as a place holder.Your credit card won’t be charged before you dine with us unless you either don’t show up for your reservation or cancel after 11:59 PM Eastern Time on the day before your arrival. So, we encourage you to keep your reservation and enjoy your dining experience!, For more convenience, add a credit card to your profile. That makes the process of booking reservations proceed even more quickly for you.
Why don’t some of my dining reservations appear in the My Plans or My Reservations sections of My Disney Experience?
Your dining reservations are tied to a specific Disney account. It is possible that you made the reservation on another account or you were not signed in when you made the reservations. They also might not be showing up if you made your reservations over the phone, at the hotel concierge or in person at the restaurant.Link an existing dining reservation to your Disney account, . You will have to sign in to link the reservation.If you are still unable to see your dining reservations, please call (407) 939-3463. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
Can I book more than one reservation for the same meal period?
No. Guests are not permitted to book dining reservations within 2 hours of another reservation. This constraint helps us provide you with the most choices and availability when making your dining plans.Other Important Details, Reservation availability for select Walt Disney World restaurants typically begins each day at approximately 5:45 AM.Please be aware that if you cancel a restaurant reservation, your previously scheduled reservation time will immediately be made available to another Guest.All newly introduced dining events—such as special dining experiences and dessert parties—can typically be booked beginning at 7:00 AM on the day their offers become available.
Is FastPass+ service like a restaurant reservation? Do I have to show up at a specific time for an attraction?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.No—it’s better! For extra convenience, you are assigned an arrival window—usually one hour long—for each attraction you select. Show up any time that you wish during this window. Don’t worry about rushing to finish up a meal or getting delayed at another show or attraction.When it is within your designated arrival window time and you are ready to visit an attraction, all you need to do is proceed to the attraction, go to the FastPass+ entrance and touch your MagicBand,  or card to the touch point.While attractions usually offer a one-hour arrival window, other experiences like shows and parades may require you to arrive during a more specific timeframe.Valid theme park admission is required.Learn more about FastPass+ service,  or make FastPass+ selections for attractions and entertainment.

Yes. You can cancel your dining reservation online, . How do I cancel my hotel reservation?

Why do you ask for the age of my children when I am shopping for hotel rooms or theme park tickets? 
We use your children’s ages to provide you with the most appropriate available offer. The prices of our packages, hotel rooms and theme park tickets are based on the ages of your party members. Guest ages also determine the maximum number of occupants of some Disney Resort hotel rooms.
Where can I find my hotel or package reservation confirmation number?
View an existing reservation online on the My Reservations page in My Disney Experience,  to check the confirmation number. You will need to sign into your account.When you make a new reservation online, you will see your confirmation number on both the online confirmation page and your confirmation email. If you make your reservation over the phone, your booking agent will verbally provide you with a confirmation number—you may also receive either a confirmation email or receive a letter in the mail with the confirmation number.Please keep your confirmation number for reference. If you wish to view a reservation online that you made over the phone, you may need to link your reservation to My Disney Experience,  by entering your confirmation number and the phone number that you used to make the call. After you do so, the reservation will show up on the My Reservations page to allow you to easily reference it in the future.
I’d like to visit Walt Disney World Resort, but heard there is a new payment card policy with an authorization hold. How much—and how long—is the hold?
On the day of arrival, Resort hotels will place an authorization hold on your card for any balance due on the reservation—plus $100 for estimated incidental expenses. If your spending exceeds the original $100 hold, additional incremental holds will automatically be obtained. The authorization holds on the card will not exceed the current balance due plus $100.Payment is processed for the balance due on the account after checkout. For reservations longer than 5 days, the card on file will be charged the current balance on the Resort folio(s) every fifth day of your stay and after checkout. In general, charges will be settled and posted to the card within 1 to 2 days after checkout day.You will only be charged for what you actually spent and any authorization holds in excess of the balance due will be released after checkout day.This policy doesn’t change your booking terms and conditions. If you’ve booked a reservation that must be prepaid—or if you’ve opted to provide full payment in advance of your stay—the balance due upon check-in is zero dollars, and only the $100 authorization hold for estimated incidental expenses will be placed on your card.For a reservation that is not prepaid, an authorization hold for the remainder of any balance due on the reservation and an additional $100 for estimated incidental expenses will be placed on your card upon the scheduled arrival date. Additional authorization holds will automatically be placed on the card, through and until the end of your checkout day, as incidental expenditures exceed the amount previously authorized to the card.Explore Walt Disney World Resort Hotels, , or view the full Payment Card Policy.

What is the Online Check-in Service?
The Online Check-in service is a convenient option that starts your check-in process online. As a component of the Direct-to-Room service, , Online Check-in can help Disney Resort hotel,  Guests reduce registration time and simplify their arrival—while still enjoying a magical Disney welcome.When you use the Direct-to-Room service, you provide us in advance of your arrival with information typically collected during a traditional check-in at the Front Desk. On arrival day, you’ll receive notifications on your mobile device (based on communication preferences you have opted into) with real-time updates, including when your room is ready and what your room number is. When your room is ready, use the Resort hotel map in the app to find your room. Then unlock your door with your MagicBand, or use the Unlock Door feature on the app.Begin your check-in to go directly to your room by linking your Disney Resort hotel reservation,  to your Disney Account. Once linked, view your reservation on the “My Plans”,  page and select “Start Check-in.” Or view your reservation from the “My Plans” screen in the My Disney Experience app.

What are the benefits of the Travel Protection Plan?
The Travel Protection Plan helps protect you and your family for unexpected covered losses from the moment that you step out of your front door until the moment you safely arrive back home. The Travel Protection Plan provides coverage if you cancel or interrupt your Walt Disney World, Disneyland or Aulani, a Disney Resort and Spa package for covered reasons described in the plan such as illness or injury. If you cancel due to a covered reason, the Travel Protection Plan will provide a refund for the prepaid, nonrefundable travel package, including the cost of airfare that is scheduled for travel within 7 days of the travel package.The Travel Protection Plan also provides coverage for covered losses while traveling, such as trip interruption, trip and baggage delays, baggage protection and medical expense protection (including emergency medical transportation). In addition, the Travel Protection Plan contains non-insurance services for 24-hour worldwide emergency assistance (provided by LiveTravel).To view the terms, conditions and exclusions, visit: www.affinitytravelcert.com/docs/DSP01, If you have questions, please call (844) 203-3123 to speak with a representative from Aon Affinity, the program administrator.To purchase Travel Protection, please select the "Add Travel Protection" option when booking your vacation package, . Travel Protection may also be added to your reservation by calling Walt Disney World Resort at (407) 939-1936. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Travel Protection Plan can be purchased any time prior to final payment for your trip.Aon Affinity is the brand name for the brokerage and program administration of Affinity Insurance Services, Inc. Is Disney’s Magical Express service available to international travelers?
Yes. Disney's Magical Express service,  is available to Guests staying at select Walt Disney World Resort hotels, , whether they are international or domestic travelers.Disney’s Magical Express service is a complimentary roundtrip service that whisks you and your luggage between Orlando International Airport and your Disney Resort hotel via a deluxe motor coach.Disney’s Magical Express service will no longer provide luggage delivery for those arriving to and departing from the airport. Resort Airline Check-In Service is also no longer available.Guests who choose to use Disney’s Magical Express service will be responsible for picking up any of their checked luggage from the airport’s baggage claim area, so that it can be loaded onto the motorcoach to their Disney Resort hotel. Disney’s Magical Express service is located at the Main Terminal Building in Terminal B, Level 1 in the Ground Transportation area.Please know that your luggage will travel with you to your Disney Resort hotel.Luggage assistance will be available at the front of your Disney Resort hotel, including luggage storage and/or transport to the room.Upon your departure, please ensure your luggage is with you and is loaded onto the motorcoach so you can check it in with your airline once you reach the airport.
I’m an international Guest with a Disney's Magical Express service reservation, but I did not receive information about the service prior to arrival. What should I do when I arrive at Orlando International Airport?
Upon exiting your aircraft, enter the U.S. Immigration checkpoint. After retrieving your luggage, proceed to the Customs checkpoint.When exiting the Customs area, keep your checked bags with you to travel on the motorcoach.Take the train to the Main Terminal Building where you will arrive on Level 3. Disney's Magical Express service is located in Terminal B, Level 1. Guests arriving in Terminal A of the airport are advised to cross to Terminal B before proceeding down to Level 1. Upon arrival at Disney’s Magical Express welcome center, please let us know if you will need assistance boarding the motorcoach.Disney’s Magical Express service will no longer provide luggage delivery for those arriving to and departing from the airport. Resort Airline Check-In Service is also no longer available.The luggage you have brought with you since the Immigration Checkpoint can be loaded onto the motorcoach to travel with you to your Disney Resort hotel.Luggage assistance will be available at the front of your Disney Resort hotel, including luggage storage and/or transport to the room.Upon your departure, please ensure your luggage is with you and is loaded onto the motorcoach so you can check it in with your airline once you reach the airport.View a map of Orlando International Airport,  or learn more about Disney's Magical Express.
As an international traveler, do I have to claim my luggage at the airport to use Disney's Magical Express service?
Yes. If the Orlando International Airport is your first point of entry into the United States, please follow the U.S. Customs & Border Protection process and claim your luggage upon disembarking the airplane.If you have already completed the U.S. Customs & Border Protection process by entry into the United States through another United States city, proceed directly to baggage claim to claim your luggage, and then, proceed to Disney's Magical Express in Terminal B, Level 1 to board your motorcoach.Take the train to the Main Terminal Building where you will arrive on Level 3. Disney's Magical Express service is located in Terminal B, Level 1. Guests arriving in Terminal A of the airport are advised to cross to Terminal B before proceeding down to Level 1. Upon arrival at Disney’s Magical Express Service, please let us know if you will need assistance boarding the motorcoach.Disney’s Magical Express service will no longer provide luggage delivery for those arriving to and departing from the airport. Resort Airline Check-In Service is also no longer available.Your luggage can be loaded onto the motorcoach to travel with you to your Disney Resort hotel.Luggage assistance will be available at the front of your Disney Resort hotel, including luggage storage and/or transport to the room.Upon your departure, please ensure your luggage is with you and is loaded onto the motorcoach so you can check it in with your airline once you reach the airport.Learn more about Disney's Magical Express service.
I am taking a Disney’s Magical Express motorcoach back to Orlando International Airport. Where is the motorcoach drop-off location?
Disney’s Magical Express motorcoaches drop off at Orlando International Airport, providing access to all airline ticket counters and departure gates. View a map of Orlando International Airport.The day before you check out, you’ll receive a transportation notice advising you of the motorcoach departure time, which will be approximately 3 hours prior to your scheduled departure time for domestic flights and 4 hours prior to your scheduled departure time for international flights. If you are not checking your luggage to the motorcoach departure location. Bell service luggage assistance is available upon request.Be sure to have your Transportation Notice on hand when it’s time for your Disney’s Magical Express departure. Your motorcoach driver will collect the Transportation Notice prior to boarding. Please note: MagicBands cannot be used to check in for your trip from your Disney Resort hotel to Orlando International Airport.If you do not receive this information, please speak to your Disney Resort hotel Concierge or call (866) 599-0951. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Learn more about Disney’s Magical Express.

I am a citizen of the United Kingdom or Ireland. What should I know about traveling to the United States?
Visit the following government websites for the latest information to help you plan your trip from the United Kingdom or Ireland to the United States.Citizens of the United Kingdom, Please check the United Kingdom government website,  for up-to-date information—including advisories on the Visa Waiver Programme (VWP), Electronic System for Travel Authorisation (ESTA) application and valuable travel tips.Citizens of Ireland, Please check the Irish Department of Foreign Affairs and Trade website,  for up-to-date information—including advisories on visas, travel insurance, safety, local laws, customs and climate.
I’m traveling to Walt Disney World Resort from the United Kingdom. What is ATOL and how will it affect my trip?
ATOL is the Air Travel Organisers’ License, issued to the Walt Disney Travel Company by the United Kingdom Civil Aviation Authority (CAA). This ensures that any money paid to us for an air-inclusive holiday package is safe and that you will not be stranded abroad.On disneyworld.com, only holiday packages that include flights are financially protected by the ATOL scheme. When you pay, you will be supplied with an ATOL Certificate. Please ask for the certificate and check to ensure that all information listed on it is correct.Review the Walt Disney Travel Company booking terms and conditions,  or learn more about the ATOL Certificate and its financial protection.
I’m traveling to Walt Disney World Resort. What is a codeshare flight?
A codeshare is a deal struck between 2 or more airlines to carry each other's passengers. This arrangement allows carriers to provide passengers with a much wider choice of destinations. The flight number of the airline you book will appear on your ticket, and the operating carrier should appear in your flight details.
How can I ensure a pet-friendly loop for my campsite at Disney's Fort Wilderness Resort?
When booking your campsite, you may request a pet-friendly loop for an additional $5.00 per night.If you make your reservations online, , select the “Add” button in the “Room and Amenity Requests” section. You will then be able to request a pet-friendly loop.Please note: Pets are not allowed in pop-up trailers or tents.Learn more about The Campsites at Disney's Fort Wilderness Resort.
Why do you ask for the age of my children when I am shopping for hotel rooms or theme park tickets? 
We use your children’s ages to provide you with the most appropriate available offer. The prices of our packages, hotel rooms and theme park tickets are based on the ages of your party members. Guest ages also determine the maximum number of occupants of some Disney Resort hotel rooms.

Do you have any pet-friendly hotels?
Yes. As part of an ongoing pilot program, 4 of our Disney Resort hotels have designated dog-friendly accommodations, including:Disney’s Art of Animation Resort, Disney Port Orleans Resort – Riverside, Disney’s Yacht Club Resort, The Cabins at Fort Wilderness Resort, These rooms have easy access to outdoor walkways for exercise and to green spaces with pet relief areas. Upon arrival, dogs and their owners will be greeted with a complimentary Pluto’s Welcome Kit. At this time, dogs are the only pets allowed, with a maximum of 2 permitted per Guest room. Dogs are expected to be well-behaved, leashed in public areas and properly vaccinated. While certain floors or sections of these Disney Resort hotels are designated as dog-friendly, the majority of areas remain canine-free to protect Guests with allergies. Other than service animals, dogs are not permitted in theme parks, water parks or common areas such as restaurants, pools and recreational spaces. For more information, call (407) 934-7639. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.

If a member of my party is afraid of dogs or has allergies, what will you do to accommodate us?
As part of this pilot program, certain floors or sections of four hotels (out of our 26 Walt Disney World Resort hotels) are designated as dog-friendly, while a majority of areas remain canine-free to accommodate guests with allergies or other needs. This means approximately 250 rooms, or less than 1 percent of a total room inventory of 28,000 rooms, are designated as dog-friendly. In addition, we have a thorough cleaning process for our rooms and will work to accommodate your individual needs.
Can you guarantee that my room will be dog-free?
We can guarantee your request to stay outside of the designated dog-friendly areas at one of these four resorts. These dog-friendly Disney Resort hotels are: Disney’s Art of Animation Resort, Disney Port Orleans Resort – Riverside, Disney’s Yacht Club Resort, The Cabins at Fort Wilderness Resort, The overwhelming number of hotels and hotel rooms at Walt Disney World Resort are not part of this pilot program, which affects approximately 250 rooms, or less than 1 percent of a total hotel inventory of 28,000 rooms. If you prefer to stay at a hotel that is not dog-friendly, there are several other Walt Disney World Resort hotels,  to choose from. 
Do I need to provide veterinary documentation for my dog?
Yes. You must be able to provide documentation that your dog’s vaccinations and inoculations are up to date, upon request.
Will there be designated pet relief areas at each dog-friendly Disney Resort hotel?
Yes. Green spaces have been identified as pet relief areas. Please note these areas are not under cover. As the owner, you will be responsible for cleaning up after your pet.Remember, dogs are not allowed in public areas around the Resort, and are expected to be on leash between your Guest room and the outdoor relief area. 
Is there a charge for staying at a dog-friendly Disney Resort hotel with my dogs?
Yes. If you are staying at Disney’s Art of Animation Resort, Disney Port Orleans Resort – Riverside,  or The Cabins at Disney's Fort Wilderness Resort, , a charge of $50 per night plus tax will be applied to the room account. If you are staying at Disney’s Yacht Club Resort, , a charge of $75 per night plus tax will be applied to the room account.
Are Disney Transportation options available for service animals and pets at Walt Disney World Resort?
Select Disney transportation options are available for Guests traveling with service animals and pets at Walt Disney World Resort.Service Animals, Service animals may accompany their owners on Disney Transportation motorcoaches, monorails and watercraft.Pets, Pet dogs may accompany their owners on internal buses at Disney’s Fort Wilderness Resort & Campground,  and Disney’s Port Orleans Resort, . No other pets are permitted on these buses.Only service animals are allowed on Disney Transportation motorcoaches, monorails or watercraft.
Are service animals and pets permitted on Disney’s Magical Express motorcoaches?
Disney’s Magical Express is available for Guests traveling with service animals and pets at Walt Disney World Resort.Service Animals, Service animals may travel on the Disney’s Magical Express motorcoach in the passenger cabin with their owners.Pets, Pet dogs may travel to a dog-friendly resort on the Disney’s Magical Express motorcoach in the passenger cabin while in a pet carrier. The pet carrier must be provided by the owner, and it must be able to fit safely in a seat on the motorcoach.No other pets are permitted in the passenger cabin or the storage compartment.Learn more about Disney’s Magical Express,  or accommodations for Guests with disabilities at Walt Disney World Resort.

Can I cancel or modify my theme park ticket or vacation package?
Tickets and packages at Walt Disney World Resort are nontransferable and nonrefundable. You cannot cancel or get a refund for a ticket or package, but in some cases you can use unexpired theme park tickets for a future vacation.However, be aware that unless you purchased the No Expiration Option, theme park tickets purchased after 2004 expire 14 days after their first use. While the No Expiration Option is no longer available, if you have previously purchased theme park tickets with the No Expiration Option, your tickets will still be honored.Hurricane Exception,  In the event that a hurricane warning is issued by the National Hurricane Center for the Orlando area—or for your place of residence—within 7 days of your scheduled arrival date, you may be able to reschedule or cancel your ticket or vacation package. See our Hurricane Policy,  for details.Also, some open-air events and dining offerings may be rescheduled or cancelled in the event of severe or inclement weather—please inquire at the time of your ticket purchase. Water parks and certain events, experiences and attractions are also subject to rehabilitation, seasonal and weather closures. Have Questions? We Have Answers!  If you have additional questions about your theme park tickets, please check with Guest Relations at the theme parks or call (407) 939-1289. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.

I purchased theme park tickets years ago and never used them. Are they still valid?
Walt Disney World Resort continues to honor all unexpired theme park tickets with remaining admission days.However, be aware that unless you purchased the No Expiration Option, theme park tickets purchased after 2004 expire 14 days after their first use. While the No Expiration Option is no longer available, if you have previously purchased theme park tickets with the No Expiration Option, your tickets will still be honored.If you have additional questions about your specific theme park tickets, please check with Guest Relations,  at the theme parks or call (407) 939-1289. Do I have to link all of my tickets to my Disney account?
No. However, to take full advantage of MyMagic+, , we recommend that Guests link their tickets,  to their Disney account.Linking a ticket to your Disney account allows you to conveniently access your tickets through your MagicBand or card, , so you don’t have to worry about bringing multiple pieces of paper with you on your vacation. You can link theme park tickets, water park tickets, special event tickets and annual passes.Don’t worry! If you lose your MagicBand or card and it is linked to your Disney account, you do not also lose your tickets. You can request a replacement MagicBand or card,  and access your tickets through the new MagicBand or card. Replacement MagicBands may be subject to a fee.Please hold on to any annual pass that you link to your Disney account, as you may need to show your pass for theme park complimentary standard parking (if your pass includes parking) and food and merchandise discounts—along with a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.

Effective April 4, 2016, Disney Vacation Club Members who do not purchase their ownership interest directly from Disney Vacation Development, Inc. will not have access to Member discounts on applicable ticket media.

What proof of residence will I need to provide in order to purchase a Florida Resident park ticket or annual pass?
You’ll need to provide proof of a Florida residential address in order to purchase a Florida Resident park ticket or annual pass. For each ticket or pass purchased for an adult, you may provide any of the following:Valid Florida driver’s license (must have a Florida address), Valid Florida state-issued ID card (must have a Florida address), Valid Florida-based military ID, *For your convenience, Florida residents with any of the above listed identification can now verify their residency online, which means you can bypass Guest Relations and go straight to the parks! Simply fill out the “Your Florida Resident Information” form upon check-out when you purchase tickets through Disneyworld.com or complete the “Customize Your Tickets” step when you purchase through the My Disney Experience app.If you do not have one of the IDs indicated above, then you must provide one of the following—dated within the past 2 months—evidencing a Florida residential address, along with a corresponding picture ID (passport, driver's license, state identification card):Proof of Current Mortgage, You may use a monthly mortgage statement from within the past 2 months; it may not be more than 2 months old. Deeds, mortgage contracts, mortgage payment booklets and leases are not accepted.Bills, Policies or Registration, Current homeowner's insurance policy or bill, Current automobile registration, insurance policy or bill, Current Utility bill (power / phone / cable / water), Bills can be no more than 2 months old (P.O. Boxes are not accepted as proof of residency), Mail, Mail from financial institutions, including checking, savings or investment account statements, Mail from federal, state, county or city government agencies, Mail can be no more than 2 months old (P.O. Boxes are not accepted as proof of residency), Additional members of the same household must only provide proof of same residential address.Current statements and bills printed from electronic versions are accepted, along with electronic bills provided via smart phones and tablet devices.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.
How do I give someone theme park tickets as a gift?
It’s easy to give Walt Disney World theme park tickets as a gift. Enter the first and last name of the Guest and make your purchase.Please keep in mind that gift orders will not be available immediately. It may take up to 24 hours after you received your email order confirmation before the recipient can pick up their tickets.Picking Up Gift Tickets, To pick up the ticket order at the park Main Entrance ticket window:The gift recipient will need to present the gift receipt and a valid government-issued photo ID.The name you provided for the gift recipient must match the name on the ID. If the recipient is a minor, the minor's parent or legal guardian will need to accompany the minor and present a valid government-issued photo ID.Ready to give some magic? Select your tickets!
How do I renew someone else's annual pass as a gift?

You must both be present to complete the renewal of the pass.Learn more about annual passes.
When can I use my theme park ticket?
Walt Disney World Resort theme park tickets are valid for admission beginning on the selected start date and must be used within the valid use period provided at the time of purchase. Here are the details:1-day,  – The ticket expires on the selected start date.2-day,  – The ticket expires 4 days after the selected start date.3-day,  – The ticket expires 5 days after the selected start date.4-day,  – The ticket expires 7 days after the selected start date.5-day,  – The ticket expires 8 days after the selected start date.6-day,  – The ticket expires 9 days after the selected start date.7-day,  – The ticket expires 10 days after the selected start date.8-day,  – The ticket expires 12 days after the selected start date.9-day,  – The ticket expires 13 days after the selected start date.10-day,  – The ticket expires 14 days after the selected start date.For example, a 6-day base ticket with a start date of November 1 is valid any 6 days from November 1 to November 9.Selection of the Park Hopper Option,  for same-day admission to more than one theme park is subject to the validity windows listed above.Selection of the Water Park and Sports Option,  to include visits to Disney water parks and other attractions—along with admission to one theme park per day—adds another day to your valid use period. For example, a 6-day Water Park and Sports Option ticket with a start date of November 1 is valid any 6 days from November 1 to November 10.Selection of the Park Hopper Plus Option,  to include visits to Disney water parks and other attractions—along with same-day admission to more than one theme park— adds another day to your valid use period. For example, a 6-day Park Hopper Plus Option ticket with a start date of November 1 is valid any 6 days from November 1 to November 10.Disney Theme Park Tickets Purchased as Part of a Walt Disney Travel Company Package, Tickets purchased as part of a Walt Disney Travel Company room and ticket package are valid for admission beginning on the date of check-in and must be used by the date of check-out, or in accordance with the validity windows listed above—whichever period is longer.Learn more about tickets.Additional Ticket Information, The amount paid for an unused, expired ticket may be applied towards the purchase of a new ticket at the current price so long as the new ticket purchase price is equal to or greater than the amount paid for the original ticket.Unless otherwise stated, tickets are not valid for separately priced activities or events. Admission is subject to capacity closures and to other restrictions.Purchasing Tickets, Don’t have theme park tickets yet? Purchase your tickets now.
I’m an Annual Passholder. How often will I receive the Mickey Monitor newsletter?
The Mickey Monitor newsletter is mailed out every February, May, August and November, and each edition includes additional benefits and program updates.  Remember: only one newsletter will be sent per active Walt Disney World Passholder household, and is exclusively available in the United States and Puerto Rico.
I purchased tickets to a special event—like Mickey's Not-So-Scary Halloween Party or Mickey's Very Merry Christmas Party—and selected Print at Home eTickets as the delivery method, but I never received the tickets. Who should I contact?
We apologize that you did not receive your eTicket. When you purchased your tickets from disneyworld.com, you should have been given the option to print or download the tickets as PDF files, . The PDF files should also have been emailed to you. Please double check your computer and email to make sure you do not already have the ticket files.If you’ve confirmed that you do not have a copy of the ticket files, please visit any Walt Disney World theme park ticket window or Disney Springs , Guest Relations.
I ordered tickets, but they did not arrive as scheduled. Who should I contact?
Email ticket.inquiries@disneyworld.com,  or call (407) 566-4985. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Although Walt Disney World Resort can sometimes get your order to you faster than the required number of days, 14 days is allotted for the processing, handling and shipping of your tickets.Please Check Our Property Rules, We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort property rules,  before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions. We regularly update our property rules to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience at Walt Disney World Resort.
Can I use more than one credit card to purchase tickets on disneyworld.com? 
You are only able to use one credit card per transaction.Purchases on disneyworld.com may be made with the following forms of payment: , Visa, MasterCard, American Express, Discover Card, Diners Club Charge Card, JCB (Japan Credit Bureau), Disney Gift Card, Disney Rewards Dollars, Disney® Visa® Card , Disney® Visa® Card is available to United States residents only.
How can I determine if a promotional offer is still available?
View the current special offers for Walt Disney World tickets, Disney Resort hotels, vacation packages and more.If you do not see the offer that you are looking for, but you believe that it may still be valid, please call (407) 939-7675. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Some offers may be specific to you—for example, if you received an offer by mail or email. If you are inquiring about such an offer, please follow the instructions related to the offer.
I have a MagicBand and tickets that are both linked to my Disney account. Do I still need to bring the tickets to Walt Disney World Resort?
No. If you have an active MagicBand, , you do not need to present your ticket at the theme park Main Entrance after linking both to your Disney account. Any active MagicBand or card linked to your Disney account will be able to access your linked theme park admission.However, please hold on to any annual pass that you link to your Disney account, as you may need to show your pass for theme park complimentary standard parking (if your pass includes parking) and food and merchandise discounts—along with a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.Linking a ticket to your Disney account allows you to conveniently access your tickets through your MagicBand or card, so you don’t have to worry about bringing multiple pieces of paper with you during your visit. You can link theme park tickets, water park tickets, special event tickets and annual passes.Don’t worry! If you lose your MagicBand or card and it is linked to your Disney account, you do not also lose your tickets. You can request a replacement MagicBand or card,  and access your tickets through the new MagicBand or card. Replacement MagicBands may be subject to a fee.Link a ticket to your Disney account.
What are the advantages of linking a ticket to my Disney account?
Linking a ticket to your Disney account,  allows you to conveniently access your tickets through your MagicBand or card, , so you don’t have to worry about bringing multiple pieces of paper with you during your visit. You can link theme park tickets, water park tickets, special event tickets and annual passes.Don’t worry! If you lose your MagicBand or card and it is linked to your Disney account, you do not also lose your tickets. You can request a replacement MagicBand or card,  and access your tickets through the new MagicBand or card. Replacement MagicBands may be subject to a fee.Please hold on to any annual pass that you link to your Disney account, as you may need to show your pass for theme park complimentary standard parking (if your pass includes parking) and food and merchandise discounts—along with a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.Link a ticket to your Disney account.
Am I able to link all of the tickets that I need for my visit to Walt Disney World Resort to my Disney account?
In many cases, yes. Most theme park and special event tickets can be linked to your Disney account. However, some events, entertainment and other offerings—like movies at AMC Disney Springs 24, —require physical tickets.Please hold on to any annual pass that you link to your Disney account, as you may need to show your pass for theme park complimentary standard parking (if your pass includes parking) and food and merchandise discounts—along with a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.Linking a ticket to your Disney account allows you to conveniently access your tickets through your MagicBand or card, , so you don’t have to worry about bringing multiple pieces of paper with you during your visit.Don’t worry! If you lose your MagicBand or card and it is linked to your Disney account, you do not also lose your tickets. You can request a replacement MagicBand or card,  and access your tickets through the new MagicBand or card. Replacement MagicBands may be subject to a fee.Purchase a ticket,  or link a ticket to your Disney account. 
I linked a ticket my Disney account. Will the ticket still expire?
Yes. Your theme park tickets,  will expire as usual. Tickets maintain the same terms and conditions—including the expiration policy—as they had before you linked them to your Disney account.Most theme park tickets expire 14 days after the date of their first use, but please be sure to check the specific terms and conditions for your ticket to confirm their expiration policy.If you have questions about when your tickets will expire, please ask at a Guest Relations,  location at Walt Disney World Resort or call (407) 939-1289. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Linking a ticket to your Disney account allows you to conveniently access your tickets through your MagicBand or card, , so you don’t have to worry about bringing multiple pieces of paper with you during your visit. You can link theme park tickets, water park tickets, special event tickets and annual passes.Please hold on to any annual pass that you link to your Disney account, as you may need to show your pass for theme park complimentary standard parking (if your pass includes parking) and food and merchandise discounts—along with a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.Link a ticket to your Disney account.
After I link a ticket to my Disney account, can I reassign the ticket to someone else?
Yes. If the ticket has not yet been used, you can reassign a ticket to another person on your Family & Friends list, . To do so, visit the My Reservations,  section of My Disney Experience, , locate the ticket you wish to reassign and select the “Reassign Ticket” link to the right of the ticket.Tickets can be reassigned until their first usage. Once they are used, tickets cannot be reassigned.To use tickets for theme park entry, all Guests must have an active MagicBand or card, . If you have tickets linked to your Disney account but you do not have an active MagicBand or card, please visit any theme park ticket window or Guest Relations,  location when you arrive at Walt Disney World Resort.Visit My Reservations to view and reassign unused tickets.
Does the Park Hopper Option provide admission to the water parks?
No. Disney Theme Park Tickets,  with the Park Hopper Option do not include admission to the Disney water parks—, Disney's Blizzard Beach Water Park,  and Disney's Typhoon Lagoon Water Park.However, Disney Theme Park Tickets with the Water Park and Sports Option or Park Hopper Plus Option do include a certain number of admissions to the water parks—based on the number of days in your ticket or package. If you wish to visit a Disney water park, we recommend that you add the Water Park and Sports Option or Park Hopper Plus Option to your ticket. Individual admission tickets are also available at the Main Entrance of each water park.Please Check Our Property Rules, We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort property rules,  before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions. We regularly update our property rules to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience at Walt Disney World Resort.
Do Annual Passholders receive discounts on theme park or water park tickets for other people?
View the latest Passholder discounts—including the complete terms for booking and redeeming discounts.Learn more about annual passes,  or purchase a new pass.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.

I’m a Florida resident and I purchased an Annual Pass with the Monthly Payment Program. Can I pay off my balance at any time?
Yes. If you are a Florida Resident and purchased an annual pass using the monthly payment program, you may pay off your balance in its entirety at any time without penalty by calling Passholder Payment Services at (888) 701-4100. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.You can also pay at the ticket booth of any theme park in Walt Disney World Resort or at Disney Springs Guest Relations.Learn more about Annual Passes,  or our Monthly Payment Program for Florida residents.
I purchased an Annual Pass using the Monthly Payment Program for Florida residents. Can I change my credit or debit card on file during the payment period?
Yes. You can change the card used for your monthly payments at any time by visiting a Walt Disney World Guest Relations location or by contacting Passholder Payment Services at (888) 701-4100. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.If you are issued a new card during the payment period, be sure to update your card on file.Learn more about Annual Passes,  or our Monthly Payment Program for Florida residents.
I wish to link a ticket to my Disney account, but I do not see the ID Number on my ticket. What should I do?
Please double-check the ticket to be sure that it does not include the ID Number. Check both the front and the back.Some tickets may not include the necessary information to link your ticket to your Disney account, . To link these tickets, please visit the Guest Relations,  locations at the theme park Main Entrance or call us at (407) 939-1289. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Theme park tickets,  can be linked to your Disney account—including tickets with options such as the Park Hopper and Park Hopper Plus Options. In addition, water park tickets, special event tickets and Annual Passes can be linked to your Disney account.If you purchased your theme park tickets before 2005, and they are still valid for admission, you may still be able to link them to your Disney account. If you have a valid ticket from before 2005, please ask for help at the Guest Relations location at the Main Entrance of our theme parks.Link a ticket to your Disney account.
What proof of residence will I need to provide in order to purchase a Florida Resident park ticket or annual pass?
You’ll need to provide proof of a Florida residential address in order to purchase a Florida Resident park ticket or annual pass. For each ticket or pass purchased for an adult, you may provide any of the following:Valid Florida driver’s license (must have a Florida address), Valid Florida state-issued ID card (must have a Florida address), Valid Florida-based military ID, *For your convenience, Florida residents with any of the above listed identification can now verify their residency online, which means you can bypass Guest Relations and go straight to the parks! Simply fill out the “Your Florida Resident Information” form upon check-out when you purchase tickets through Disneyworld.com or complete the “Customize Your Tickets” step when you purchase through the My Disney Experience app.If you do not have one of the IDs indicated above, then you must provide one of the following—dated within the past 2 months—evidencing a Florida residential address, along with a corresponding picture ID (passport, driver's license, state identification card):Proof of Current Mortgage, You may use a monthly mortgage statement from within the past 2 months; it may not be more than 2 months old. Deeds, mortgage contracts, mortgage payment booklets and leases are not accepted.Bills, Policies or Registration, Current homeowner's insurance policy or bill, Current automobile registration, insurance policy or bill, Current Utility bill (power / phone / cable / water), Bills can be no more than 2 months old (P.O. Boxes are not accepted as proof of residency), Mail, Mail from financial institutions, including checking, savings or investment account statements, Mail from federal, state, county or city government agencies, Mail can be no more than 2 months old (P.O. Boxes are not accepted as proof of residency), Additional members of the same household must only provide proof of same residential address.Current statements and bills printed from electronic versions are accepted, along with electronic bills provided via smart phones and tablet devices.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.

Bring a printed copy of your certificate along with a photo ID to any Walt Disney World theme park ticket window for redemption. If you purchased an annual pass or used our Monthly Payment Program for Florida residents, you will also need to bring proof of Florida residency.Each Passholder will need to be present at the ticket window to receive his or her pass.Learn more about annual passes,  or purchase an annual pass.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. We regularly update our property rules to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience at Walt Disney World Resort.
When can I renew my Annual Pass?
You can renew your Annual Pass up to 60 days before and 30 days after the pass expiration date. Keep in mind that your renewed Annual Pass will expire one year from your Anniversary Date, regardless of when you actually renew.There are 3 convenient ways to renew:Renew online, Renew at any Walt Disney World Resort theme park ticket window or Disney Springs Guest Relations location.Renew over the phone by calling (407) 560-PASS or (407) 560-7277. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.If you are renewing through the Monthly Payment Program for Florida residents, phone renewals are not available. However, you can renew online, in person at a theme park ticket window or Guest Relations location.Though the Annual Pass owner does not need to be present for renewal, each Annual Pass owner will need to be present at the ticket window to receive his or her pass.Learn more about Annual Passes,  or purchase a new Annual Pass.
Am I required to sign up for a Disney account to link a ticket to a MagicBand or card?
Yes. To link a ticket, you must have a Disney account or sign up for a new account. You do not technically link a ticket to a MagicBand or card; you link a ticket to your Disney account. You can access tickets linked to your account with any active MagicBand or card that is also linked to the account.Once you’ve signed up for a Disney account, you’ll find that it’s quick and easy to access and manage your tickets in the My Reservations,  section of My Disney Experience, . My Reservations also conveniently lists the Resort hotel reservations, vacation packages and dining reservations that you purchased or reserved on disneyworld.com.Create a new Disney account,  or link a ticket to your Disney account.

Yes, Passholders enjoy exclusive events, special offers and valuable discounts on select options including dining, merchandise, recreation, tours and more. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.
Do I need to purchase an admission ticket to attend an event at ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex?
Yes. Most ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex events do require the purchase of an admission ticket.Admission to some events may be included if you purchase a Park Hopper Plus Option with your Disney Theme Park Ticket.Learn more about ESPN Wide World of Sports Complex.
My Annual Pass will expire soon. Is there a discount for renewing?
Yes. As a courtesy, we offer a discount for renewing your Walt Disney World Annual Pass up to 30 days after your Anniversary Date.There are 3 convenient ways to renew your Annual Pass:Renew online, Renew at any Walt Disney World Resort theme park ticket window or Disney Springs Guest Relations location.Renew over the phone by calling (407) 560-PASS or (407) 560-7277. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.If you are renewing through the Monthly Payment Program for Florida residents, phone renewals are not available. However, you can renew online, in person at a theme park ticket window or Guest Relations location. Annual Passes can be renewed up to 60 days before and 30 days after expiration.Though the Annual Pass owner does not need to be present for renewal, each Annual Pass owner will need to be present at the ticket window to receive his or her pass.Learn more about Annual Passes,  or purchase a new Annual Pass.
I ordered theme park tickets from disneyworld.com and selected standard shipping. The site said that my order will arrive in 14 days. Will my tickets actually come in less time?
Although Walt Disney World Resort can sometimes get your order to you faster than the required number of days, 14 days is allotted for the processing, handling and shipping of your tickets.If you need tickets in less than 14 days, you may purchase your tickets when you arrive at Walt Disney World Resort.
When can I use my theme park ticket?
Walt Disney World Resort theme park tickets are valid for admission beginning on the selected start date and must be used within the valid use period provided at the time of purchase. Here are the details:1-day,  – The ticket expires on the selected start date.2-day,  – The ticket expires 4 days after the selected start date.3-day,  – The ticket expires 5 days after the selected start date.4-day,  – The ticket expires 7 days after the selected start date.5-day,  – The ticket expires 8 days after the selected start date.6-day,  – The ticket expires 9 days after the selected start date.7-day,  – The ticket expires 10 days after the selected start date.8-day,  – The ticket expires 12 days after the selected start date.9-day,  – The ticket expires 13 days after the selected start date.10-day,  – The ticket expires 14 days after the selected start date.For example, a 6-day base ticket with a start date of November 1 is valid any 6 days from November 1 to November 9.Selection of the Park Hopper Option,  for same-day admission to more than one theme park is subject to the validity windows listed above.Selection of the Water Park and Sports Option,  to include visits to Disney water parks and other attractions—along with admission to one theme park per day—adds another day to your valid use period. For example, a 6-day Water Park and Sports Option ticket with a start date of November 1 is valid any 6 days from November 1 to November 10.Selection of the Park Hopper Plus Option,  to include visits to Disney water parks and other attractions—along with same-day admission to more than one theme park— adds another day to your valid use period. For example, a 6-day Park Hopper Plus Option ticket with a start date of November 1 is valid any 6 days from November 1 to November 10.Disney Theme Park Tickets Purchased as Part of a Walt Disney Travel Company Package, Tickets purchased as part of a Walt Disney Travel Company room and ticket package are valid for admission beginning on the date of check-in and must be used by the date of check-out, or in accordance with the validity windows listed above—whichever period is longer.Learn more about tickets.Additional Ticket Information, The amount paid for an unused, expired ticket may be applied towards the purchase of a new ticket at the current price so long as the new ticket purchase price is equal to or greater than the amount paid for the original ticket.Unless otherwise stated, tickets are not valid for separately priced activities or events. Admission is subject to capacity closures and to other restrictions.Purchasing Tickets, Don’t have theme park tickets yet? Purchase your tickets now.
What type of tickets can be linked to my Disney account?
Theme park tickets,  can be linked to your Disney account—including tickets with options such as the Park Hopper and Park Hopper Plus Options. In addition, water park tickets, special event tickets and annual passes can be linked to your Disney account.If you purchased your theme park tickets before 2005, and they are still valid for admission, you may still be able to link them to your Disney account. To link these older tickets, please visit the Guest Relations,  locations at the theme park Main Entrance or call us at (407) 939-1289. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Linking a ticket to your Disney account allows you to conveniently access your tickets through your MagicBand or card, , so you don’t have to worry about bringing multiple pieces of paper with you during your visit.Please hold on to any annual pass that you link to your Disney account, as you may need to show your pass for theme park complimentary standard parking (if your pass includes parking) and food and merchandise discounts—along with a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.Link a ticket to your Disney account.
Are theme park tickets transferable? May I give them to someone else to use the remaining days?
No. Once a person uses a Disney Theme Park Ticket, , all subsequent admissions are specific to that person and cannot be transferred to anyone else.If you have not yet used a ticket, you may transfer it to another person. , You may also buy a new theme park ticket online,  or at the theme park Main Entrance.Please Check Our Park Rules, We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort park rules,  before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions. We regularly update our park rules to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience at Walt Disney World Resort.

For example, a 6-day Water Park and Sports Option ticket with a start date of November 1 is valid any 6 days from November 1 to November 10.Selection of the Park Hopper Plus Option,  to include visits to Disney water parks and other attractions—along with same-day admission to more than one theme park— adds another day to your valid use period. For example, a 6-day Park Hopper Plus Option ticket with a start date of November 1 is valid any 6 days from November 1 to November 10.Disney Theme Park Tickets Purchased as Part of a Walt Disney Travel Company Package, Tickets purchased as part of a Walt Disney Travel Company room and ticket package are valid for admission beginning on the date of check-in and must be used by the date of check-out, or in accordance with the validity windows listed above—whichever period is longer.Learn more about tickets.Additional Ticket Information, The amount paid for an unused, expired ticket may be applied towards the purchase of a new ticket at the current price so long as the new ticket purchase price is equal to or greater than the amount paid for the original ticket.Unless otherwise stated, tickets are not valid for separately priced activities or events. I’ve used my tickets, but they are unexpired and still have unused days left. Can these tickets still be linked to my Disney account?
Yes. Tickets can be linked to your Disney account,  if they have been used, as long as they are unexpired and still have valid park admissions left. When you link a partially used ticket, you are asked to match the ticket to the person who previously used it for park admission. Linking a ticket to your Disney account allows you to conveniently access your tickets through your MagicBand or card, , so you don’t have to worry about bringing multiple pieces of paper with you during your visit. You can link theme park tickets, water park tickets, special event tickets and annual passes.Please hold on to any annual pass that you link to your Disney account, as you may need to show your pass for theme park complimentary standard parking (if your pass includes parking) and food and merchandise discounts—along with a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.A partially used ticket cannot be reassigned in the My Reservations,  section of My Disney Experience, . The terms and conditions of the original ticket, including expiration rules, still apply when they are linked to your Disney account. Tickets are nontransferable and must be used by the same person on all days.Link a ticket to your Disney account.
How can I determine the number of days remaining on a theme park ticket?
When you arrive at Walt Disney World Resort, please show your ticket to a Cast Member at any of the following locations:Ticket windows at theme parks and water parks, Concierge desks at Disney Resort hotels, Guest Relations at Disney Springs, If you wish to check from home, please email us at ticket.usage@disneyworld.com,  and include the following:Photograph or scan of the front and back of each ticket, Your full name, Where and when ticket was purchased, Purchaser’s name and form of payment, Phone number where you can be reached during the day, Please keep the total email size, including attachments, below 20 MB. To ensure your email is less than 20 MB, you may need to compress your images or send multiple emails.We’ll try to get back to you as soon as possible, but it normally takes 14 business days for a response.
I have linked a ticket to my Disney account. How do I use the ticket?
Once your ticket has been linked to your Disney account, , and you have matched the ticket to yourself, all you have to do is go to the theme park or water park, touch your MagicBand or card,  to the touch point at the Main Entrance and enjoy your visit!, Please hold on to any annual pass that you link to your Disney account, as you may need to show your pass for theme park complimentary standard parking (if your pass includes parking) and food and merchandise discounts—along with a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.Don’t worry! If you lose your MagicBand or card and it is linked to your Disney account, you do not also lose your tickets. You can request a replacement MagicBand or card,  and access your tickets through the new MagicBand or card. Replacement MagicBands may be subject to a fee.Visit My Reservations to view and reassign unused tickets.
I purchased a ticket that includes the Water Park Fun & More Option. Since that option is no longer being sold, can I still use my ticket?
Yes, unused and unexpired tickets that include the Water Park Fun & More Option are still valid.
Can I still purchase a ticket that includes the Water Park Fun & More Option?
Although the Water Park Fun & More Option is no longer being sold, you can purchase the Park Hopper Plus Option, which includes same-day admission to all 4 of our theme parks on each day of your ticket, plus a certain number of visits to a water park or other Walt Disney World fun.
I’m on my way to—or already at—my Resort hotel but haven’t checked in yet. Can I still participate in the Direct-to-Room service?
Yes. You can use the Direct-to-Room service anytime in advance up to and including your arrival day. However, we recommend starting the check-in process before your arrival day so you can make your vacation experience even easier and more convenient.Check-in time for all Disney Resort hotels is 3:00 PM, except for Disney Deluxe Villa Resorts, which have a check-in time of 4:00 PM.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
Can I still visit the Front Desk if I’m using the Direct-to-Room service?
Cast Members at the Front Desk are delighted to assist you with questions about your stay. Visit the Front Desk, use the Call Resort feature in the My Disney Experience app,  or tap “Front Desk” on your Disney Resort hotel room phone for personal assistance 24 hours a day. Learn more about the Front Desk.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
What is the difference between the Online Check-in and Direct-to-Room services?
Online Check-in,  is a component of the Direct-to-Room service, , offering registered Disney Resort hotel Guests at Walt Disney World Resort an opportunity to simplify their arrival while still enjoying a magical Disney welcome. The Direct-to-Room service takes the convenience of online check-in service to the next level, providing an opportunity to get to the fun faster by bypassing the Front Desk and—upon receiving a “room is ready” communication—heading straight to your room, using either a MagicBand or the My Disney Experience app,  to unlock your door.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
Can I use the Direct-to-Room service if I’m staying in a Club-Level room?
Absolutely! The Direct-to-Room service is available for all room types at participating Disney Resort hotels.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
What are the benefits of the Direct-to-Room service?
The Direct-to-Room service lets you...View your reservation, Simplify your arrival, Bypass the Front Desk⁠, Receive real-time room ready updates, including room number and arrival instructions, Have digital access to Resort hotel maps, Use your MagicBand or the My Disney Experience app to unlock your door, Begin the fun and magic of your vacation even sooner, Need anything else? You can still visit the Front Desk any time after you've arrived!, Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
How do I become eligible to use the Direct-to-Room Service?
Direct-to-Room service is a complimentary service available to all registered Disney Resort hotel Guests at Walt Disney World Resort.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
Can Guests with Disabilities Use the Direct-to-Room Service?
Of course! Guests with disabilities can also enjoy the convenience of bypassing the Front Desk and heading straight to their rooms using the Direct-to-Room service. And as always, the Front Desk Cast Members are happy to help with any requests you might have.Get an overview of the many services and access options,  available to Guests with Disabilities throughout Walt Disney World Resort.For more information, please contact Disability Services at (407) 560-2547 or email disability.services@disneyparks.com.
Where can I get help with the Direct-to-Room service?
If you are experiencing technical difficulties with the Direct-to-Room service, please check to be sure that you have the latest version of your web browser:Download Internet Explorer, Download Mozilla Firefox, Download Safari, If you’re using the latest version of your browser and you’re still unable to use the Direct-to-Room service, please call (407) 939-4357 and we will help you check in online. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
When I use the Direct-to-Room service, what sort of information do I need to provide online?
During the online check-in process, you’ll provide the same information you would typically provide to the Front Desk during a standard check-in—including a credit card for incidental charges, your arrival time, room location requests (which are subject to availability), home address and mobile phone number. We’ll also ask you to create a 4-digit personal identification number that you—and the other members of your party with charging privileges—will use to verify your identity when you make purchases and use dining entitlements at Walt Disney World Resort.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
Does participation in the Direct-to-Room service guarantee that my room will ready when I arrive at my Disney Resort hotel?
No. Rooms and campsites are available at the standard check-in time of 3:00 PM for all Disney Resort hotels, except for Disney Deluxe Villa Resorts, which have a check-in time of 4:00 PM.However, while we do not guarantee early availability, we will try to accommodate early check-in upon request.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.

Can Disney Vacation Club Members use the Direct-to-Room service when using Vacation Points or cash reservations?
Yes. Disney Vacation Club Members are able to use the Direct-to-Room service when staying at participating Disney Resort hotels.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
I arrived early, but my room's not ready yet. What can I do?
No worries! You can use your MagicBand or the Unlock Door feature on the My Disney Experience app,  to enjoy your Disney Resort hotel in a variety of areas—including the swimming pool—before your room is available.Have luggage? Drop it off with Valet, Bell Service or Luggage Assistance at the entrance of your Resort for storage until your room is ready.If you take advantage of Disney′s Magical Express transportation, , we can deliver your luggage directly to your room when it is available, so you are free to start enjoying Walt Disney World Resort. Only select Disney Resort hotels,  offer access to Disney’s Magical Express transportation.If you have a Disney dining plan, you can start using it the day you’re scheduled to arrive even before your room is available. Feel free to take advantage of quick-service locations in the hotel to utilize entitlements of the plan, such as getting a refillable drink mug, snack or a meal. To redeem, Guests need to show their MagicBand or card. If you don’t have a MagicBand, but have one awaiting your pickup at the Front Desk of your Disney Resort hotel, you can retrieve it at your convenience.*, Check-in time for all Disney Resort hotels is 3:00 PM, except for Disney Deluxe Villa Resorts, which have a check-in time of 4:00 PM. The checkout time is 11:00 AM.* Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.
How does the Direct-to-Room service work?
The Direct-to-Room service helps Disney Resort hotel Guests simplify their arrival while still enjoying a magical Disney welcome.Follow these simple steps to start enjoying the service today: Link your Disney Resort hotel reservation to your Disney Account.Use the Online Check-in service prior to arrival.On arrival day, use the My Disney Experience app to get real-time reservation updates, including a notification when your room is ready.When your room is ready, use the Resort hotel map in the app to find your room. Then unlock your door with your MagicBand, or use the Unlock Door feature on the app. Want to learn more about the Direct-to-Room service? With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.
