Is my room assigned when I initiate the Direct-to-Room service?
No. Rooms are not assigned until your arrival day. We take into consideration information you provide during the online check-in process, such as your estimated arrival time and any room location request selections (subject to availability), when assigning a room.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
I’m using the Direct-to-Room service but need help unlocking my door.
If you experience difficulties unlocking your door, get help from a Cast Member by tapping “Call Resort Hotel” on your “Resort Reservation” screen of the My Disney Experience app.
I’m visiting Walt Disney World Resort as part of a convention or group. Can I use Direct-to-Room service?
Yes. Direct-to-Room is available to members of conventions or groups.Begin the check-in process in advance of your arrival using the Direct-to-Room service on disneyworld.com,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
What is the Direct-to-Room service?
The Direct-to-Room service is a complimentary service available to all registered Disney Resort hotel Guests at Walt Disney World Resort. The service is a convenient option designed to help Guests simplify their arrival while still enjoying a magical Disney welcome. Get to the fun faster by bypassing the Front Desk⁠—plus get real-time room ready updates and even use the My Disney Experience app as a digital key!, When you use the Direct-to-Room service, you provide us in advance of your arrival with information typically collected during a traditional check-in at the Front Desk. On arrival day, you’ll receive notifications on your mobile device (based on communication preferences you have opted into) with real-time updates, including when your room is ready and what your room number is. When your room is ready, use the Resort hotel map in the app to find your room. Then unlock your door with your MagicBand, , or use the Unlock Door feature on the app.Begin your check-in to go directly to your room by linking your Disney Resort hotel reservation,  to your Disney Account. Once linked, view your reservation on the “My Plans” page,  and select “Start Check-in.” Or view your reservation from the “My Plans” screen in the My Disney Experience app.
What is the Online Check-in Service?
The Online Check-in service is a convenient option that starts your check-in process online. As a component of the Direct-to-Room service, , Online Check-in can help Disney Resort hotel,  Guests reduce registration time and simplify their arrival—while still enjoying a magical Disney welcome.When you use the Direct-to-Room service, you provide us in advance of your arrival with information typically collected during a traditional check-in at the Front Desk. On arrival day, you’ll receive notifications on your mobile device (based on communication preferences you have opted into) with real-time updates, including when your room is ready and what your room number is. When your room is ready, use the Resort hotel map in the app to find your room. Then unlock your door with your MagicBand, or use the Unlock Door feature on the app.Begin your check-in to go directly to your room by linking your Disney Resort hotel reservation,  to your Disney Account. Once linked, view your reservation on the “My Plans”,  page and select “Start Check-in.” Or view your reservation from the “My Plans” screen in the My Disney Experience app.
When can I make advance reservations for experiences at Walt Disney World Resort, such as dining reservations and available Enchanting Extras Collection experiences?
All Guests may now make advance reservations for dining and other experiences up to 60 days in advance. In addition, Disney Resort hotel Guests can make reservations up to 60 days in advance plus the length of their stay (up to 10 days).Dining reservations can be booked online, Enchanting Extras Collection experiences can be booked by calling (407) 939-6690—or (800) 800-9800 for Disney Vacation Club Members, Here are some additional details to help you plan:In-Park Dining, With the opening of Magic Kingdom park and Disney’s Animal Kingdom theme park on July 11, followed by EPCOT and Disney’s Hollywood Studios on July 15, Guests will need valid park admission and a reservation for park entry,  through the new Disney Park Pass system—as well as a dining reservation—to dine at in-park, table-service restaurants. Dining reservations do not guarantee admission to the park.Disney Resort Hotel Dining, Planning to dine at a table-service restaurant in a Disney Resort hotel? A confirmed dining reservation is required for day Guests (those not staying overnight) and is highly recommended for Guests staying overnight at a Disney Resort hotel.Disney Springs Dining, Select dining locations at Disney Springs,  are currently accepting reservations. Check availability and make reservations online now.Other Important Information, In order to foster physical distancing during this time, upon reopening, our offerings, restaurants and other experiences such as behind-the-scenes tours will be limited in capacity, while other experiences may remain closed.
My family prefers to decide what to do at breakfast each day of our park visit. To use FastPass+ service, do we have to make all our plans in advance? 
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.It’s up to you. FastPass+ service,  is great for Guests who like to make plans in advance, while also offering convenience and flexibility for Guests who prefer a more spontaneous park experience. Please keep in mind that same-day availability for certain experiences may be limited.If you are making same-day plans―and FastPass+ arrival times are available―you can secure your choices using your mobile device or at a FastPass+ kiosk in the park.Once you redeem your initial set of FastPass+ selections (or the last arrival window has passed), you can make another FastPass+ selection for the same day at an in-park kiosk,  or on your mobile device, up to park closing. After you redeem the additional FastPass+ pick, you can make more selections (one at a time), subject to availability.For a greater range of choices, we recommend you make FastPass+ selections,  early. If you prefer to be spontaneous, all attractions and Character Greetings provide standby entrances so you can decide as you go.Valid theme park admission required. FastPass+ attractions and entertainment experiences, the number of selections you can make and available arrival windows are limited. Certain MyMagic+ features and benefits require online registration.For more flexibility, use the My Disney Experience mobile app,  to select and modify FastPass+ experiences, access your vacation details and view maps and up-to-the-minute information.Make FastPass+ selections.
Can I cancel or change a FastPass+ selection?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.Yes. Keep in mind that all attractions and Character Greetings provide standby entrances so you are always free to decide as you go.In advance, you can reserve up to 3 FastPass+ experiences per day at one theme park. Once you redeem your initial set of FastPass+ selections (or the last arrival window has passed), you can make another FastPass+ selection for the same day at an in-park kiosk,  or your mobile device, up to park closing. After you redeem the additional FastPass+ pick, you can return to a kiosk to make more selections (one at a time), subject to availability.At the parks, use the My Disney Experience mobile app,  to choose and update FastPass+ selections, find real-time wait times, access your vacation details and view maps and other helpful information.Valid theme park admission required. FastPass+ attractions and entertainment experiences, the number of selections you can make and available arrival windows are limited. How does FastPass+ service let me plan for members of my family who want to enjoy different kinds of attractions and entertainment?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. Each time you request new FastPass+ selections, , you can choose the specific party members who will enjoy that set of experiences. Once you confirm those selections, you’ll be able to pick a different FastPass+ experience for those who wish to enjoy something else.If anyone in your party decides they don’t want to experience a FastPass+ selection, they are free to skip it. Please note that children under age 14 must be accompanied by a Guest age 14 or older to enter the theme parks and water parks. Once inside the parks, children under the age of 7 must be accompanied by a Guest age of 14 or older when entering an attraction.At select attractions, you can also take advantage of our Rider Switch,  option, which enables one adult to wait with children while another adult experiences the attraction. Then, the adults can switch so the other adult can experience the attraction—without having to wait in line a second time. You do not need to use FastPass+ service to use the Rider Switch option.Valid theme park admission required. FastPass+ attractions and entertainment experiences, the number of selections you can make and available arrival windows are limited. After you redeem your initial 3 selections, use the app or head to a kiosk to make another selection. If your Annual Pass permits you to visit a second park on the same day, you have the option to make additional FastPass+ selections at another park—even if you’re in a different park from your original selections!, For a greater range of choices, we recommend you make FastPass+ selections,  early. Is FastPass+ service like a restaurant reservation? Do I have to show up at a specific time for an attraction?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.No—it’s better! For extra convenience, you are assigned an arrival window—usually one hour long—for each attraction you select. Show up any time that you wish during this window. Don’t worry about rushing to finish up a meal or getting delayed at another show or attraction.When it is within your designated arrival window time and you are ready to visit an attraction, all you need to do is proceed to the attraction, go to the FastPass+ entrance and touch your MagicBand,  or card to the touch point.While attractions usually offer a one-hour arrival window, other experiences like shows and parades may require you to arrive during a more specific timeframe.Valid theme park admission is required.Learn more about FastPass+ service,  or make FastPass+ selections for attractions and entertainment.
How do I access FastPass+ service using my Annual Pass?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.If you have a valid Walt Disney World Annual Pass, please follow these simple steps to make your FastPass+ selections:Create,  or sign into,  your Disney account.Link your Annual Pass or Passes,  to your account, if you have not already done so.Access FastPass+ service.Annual Passholders can make FastPass+ selections up to 30 days in advance. Secure up to 3 FastPass+ selections for one park per day, for up to 7 days. If plans change, it’s easy to update or cancel your selections, , subject to availability.Passholders with reservations at a Walt Disney World Resort hotel,  can start making FastPass+ selections as early as 60 days prior to the check-in date―and can secure FastPass+ selections for the length of stay or up to 7 days. Please note that if your length of stay is longer than two weeks, FastPass+ selections can be made for up to 14 days.Once you redeem your initial set of FastPass+ selections (or the last arrival window has passed), you can make another FastPass+ selection for the same day at an in-park kiosk,  or on your mobile device. After you redeem the additional FastPass+ pick, you can make more selections (one at a time) up to park closing.If your Annual Pass permits you to visit a second park on the same day, after you use your initial FastPass+ selections at the first park you visit, you have the option to make additional FastPass+ selections at an in-park kiosk or using your mobile device in the second park.For a greater range of choices, we recommend you make FastPass+ selections early, . If you prefer to be spontaneous, all attractions and Character Greetings provide standby entrances so you can decide as you go.Valid theme park admission required. FastPass+ attractions and entertainment experiences, the number of selections you can make and available arrival windows are limited. Certain MyMagic+ features and benefits require online registration.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.

What happens when someone accepts my Family & Friends invitation for My Disney Experience?
Once you invite someone to connect to your Family & Friends list, that person will receive an email notification and be given the choice to accept or decline your invitation. When they accept, you will see a check mark next to their name in your Family & Friends list and you can then share the vacation planning activities in My Disney Experience. If you wish to modify what information you are sharing with other people, you can change your Family & Friends viewing permissions,  for each individual Guest by selecting the “Edit” button next to someone’s name in your Family & Friends list.View your Family & Friends list,  to invite someone to connect with you. You must sign in to My Disney Experience to view or modify your Family & Friends.
How is my information shared with the people on My Family & Friends list on disneyworld.com or the My Disney Experience app?
Each person in your Family & Friends list,  can view your full name and age on disneyworld.com or the My Disney Experience app, . People who are over 18 years of age are shown as “Age 18+”. Your contact and payment information will not be visible to people on your Family & Friends list.Depending on your settings, people connected to your Family & Friends list may also be able to see the following.My Plans, Depending on how you set permissions for each person, people connected to your Family & Friends list will be able to see all of your plans—like dining reservations, and reminders—or only view plans you have in common. The default setting is “All My Plans”.To change what plans you are sharing with someone on your Family & Friends list, , go to your Family & Friends list, select the person and select either “All My Plans” or “Only Plans We Share”.Family & Friends List, If you share your Family & Friends list, people on the list are able to see your list and invite each other to connect.To make your Family & Friends list private, go to your Family & Friends list, , select yourself and select the “Make List Private” button.Resort Hotel Reservations, People connected to your Family & Friends list who are also on your Resort hotel reservation can see your reservation information. If they are 18 years of age or older, they can view the remaining balance and make a payment.To remove someone from your reservation, please call (407) 939-1936.Disney PhotoPass Photos, People connected to your Family & Friends list can view and purchase your PhotoPass photos, videos and other digital content.To stop sharing photos with someone on your Family & Friends list, go to your Family & Friends list, , select the person and uncheck “My Disney PhotoPass Photos”.Stop Sharing All Information, If you no longer wish to share any plans or photos with someone, you can remove the person from your Family & Friends list.To remove someone from your Family & Friends list, go to your Family & Friends list, , select the person and select “Remove from This List”.
In My Disney Experience, how can multiple adults or teens make plans for a child?
In the Family & Friends,  section of My Disney Experience, , you can create a profile for a child under age 13 simply by entering the name and age. The person who creates a child’s profile will manage the profile and all the plans for that child. The child’s profile cannot be transferred to another person to manage.Only create one profile per child. Creating multiple profiles for an individual may result in issues accessing travel plans and redeeming FastPass+ selections.Any Guest age 13 and older who does not have a Disney account may create an account at any time. If you make plans on behalf of a Guest who later creates a Disney account, be sure to invite that Guest to connect with you in Family & Friends using his or her Disney account email. This allows the plans you’ve made to migrate to the other Guest’s account.Learn more about Family & Friends
I invited someone to connect to my Family & Friends list in My Disney Experience. What does the connection status of “Invite Pending” mean?
When you invite a new person to connect to your Family & Friends list,  in My Disney Experience, , they are sent an email message asking them to accept or decline your invitation. Until they respond, their status will be shown as “Invite Pending”.In most cases, all you need to do is wait. If your connection request is declined, the connection status will be shown as "Invitation Declined".If you wish to resend your invitation, select the “Invite Pending” link next to their name on your Family & Friends list.Of course, you can also call or email the person you are trying to connect to and ask them to respond to your invitation. For security reasons, we cannot provide alternative ways to contact people you invite. , If your request was declined and you believe that it should not have been, please double check the email address of the person you are inviting and confirm that it is correct. Also, keep in mind that children are unable to accept invitations to connect—their parents or guardians must do so for them.If you have repeatedly tried to connect to someone, and you are unable to do so for what you believe are technical reasons, please call (407) 939-4357. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call. 
How do I remove someone from my Family & Friends list?
To remove someone from your Family & Friends list, please follow these instructions:View your Family & Friends list in My Disney Experience. , Locate the person that you wish to remove on the list and press the “Edit” button. , You will see a page with details about the person that you wish to remove. Press the “Remove” button. , A pop-up message will appear and ask you to confirm that you wish to remove the person. Press the “Remove” button. , The above instructions will work if you are removing an adult with a separate Disney account. If you added someone to your Family & Friends list and that person does not have a separate account—for example, a young child—follow these instructions to permanently delete the person:View your Family & Friends list in My Disney Experience. , Locate the person that you wish to delete on the list and press the “Edit” button. , You will see a page with details about the person that you wish to delete. Press the “Delete” button. , A pop-up message will appear and ask you to confirm that you wish to permanently delete the person. Press the “Delete” button.Once you remove or delete someone from your Family & Friends list, you cannot undo this action. However, if they have a separate Disney account, you can request to reconnect them to your Friends & Family list.You cannot delete Guests on your Family & Friends list who have active entitlements—such as Disney dining plans. If you encounter a situation where you wish to remove or delete someone and you are unable to do so, please call (407) 939-4357. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
The words "View Only Shared Activities" appears next to one of my Family & Friends in My Disney Experience. What does this mean? 
"View Only Shared Activities" means that the permissions for that person are set so that they can only view activities you both share—including dining reservations.If you wish for a member of your Family & Friends to view all of your activities, regardless if they are involved in them, visit Family & Friends, , select the “Edit” button next to their name and change their “Plan and Share” permission to "View All Activities".
I am an Annual Passholder with a MagicBand and I have a reservation at a Disney Resort hotel. Can I get another MagicBand?
You are eligible to receive a new MagicBand,  by staying at a Disney Resort hotel with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 or purchasing one or you can customize and order a new MagicBand.If you like your current MagicBand, you can continue to use it along with your new MagicBand.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.Getting multiple MagicBands or cards does not give you multiple entitlements, such as park admission. Also, once a MagicBand or card is linked to a person, it cannot be transferred to another person. , If you have multiple MagicBands or cards, you can manage which MagicBands and Cards are active in My Profile, . Don’t see your MagicBand? You may need to link your Resort hotel reservation, link your Annual Pass,  or link the MagicBand,  to your Disney account.
Why am I required to confirm the shipping address for my MagicBand?
We want to make sure that your MagicBands,  are shipped to the correct address, so we ask you to take a second look to ensure that your address is correct. Please note that MagicBand orders cannot be shipped to all countries.If you have not yet done so, customize your MagicBand.
I am an Annual Passholder with a MagicBand and an annual pass card. What should I bring to the Walt Disney World theme parks?
Please bring your MagicBand, , annual pass card and a valid photo ID—such as a driver’s license or passport.Your MagicBand can be used for theme park admission.Your annual pass card enables you to access your Passholder entitlements—including theme park admission, food and merchandise discounts and complimentary standard theme park parking, if your pass includes parking. The pass card must be presented—along with a photo ID—at the time of purchase, when you book and when you redeem any Passholder offer.Learn more about annual passes,  or purchase a new pass.
When is the deadline for customizing my MagicBand?
If you customize your MagicBand,  with your name and favorite color as soon as possible after making your Disney Resort hotel,  reservation:If you customize your MagicBand,  at least 11 days before you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel, it will be shipped to your home.If you customize your MagicBand between 10 days and 6 days before you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel, you will receive it when you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel.If you do not customize your MagicBand until 5 days or less before your arrival, you will receive a non-customized MagicBand when you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel.MagicBand orders cannot be shipped to all countries.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.MagicBands use Radio Frequency (RF) technology and can be read by short and long-range readers located at the Walt Disney World Resort. If you prefer to use a card—which cannot be detected by long-range readers—you can request a card at your Disney Resort hotel. MagicBands and cards allow you to enter the parks, unlock Disney Resort hotel rooms and use FastPass+ service.When you customize your MagicBand, the printed name appears on the inside for your privacy.Learn about our privacy and data collection policies and the Radio Frequency (RF) technology used in MagicBands.
My MagicBand has been shipped. How long should it take to reach me?
MagicBand,  fulfillment and shipping should take about 11 days. However, it could be a few days more or less depending on factors such as holidays, weekends and inclement weather.If your MagicBands have not arrived and your visit to Walt Disney World Resort starts within 6 days, please contact us.Don’t worry! If you do not receive your MagicBands before you have to travel to Walt Disney World Resort, you will be provided with MagicBands or cards when you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.If you have not yet done so, customize your MagicBand.
Can I reuse my MagicBand or card the next time I visit Walt Disney World Resort?
Yes. If you have a MagicBand or card that you like, and it is in working condition, you can continue to use it when you return to Walt Disney World Resort.If you have multiple MagicBands or cards, you can manage which ones are active in the MagicBand section of My Profile.
How do I use my MagicBand?
Most of the time, all you need to do is touch your MagicBand against a sensor called a touch point. It’s that easy!, Your MagicBand enables you to travel lighter throughout your vacation. Use it to enter the parks, unlock your Disney Resort hotel room and buy food and merchandise. Plus, your MagicBand gives you FastPass+,  access to all the experiences you’ve selected online, so you can simply concentrate on enjoying the fun with the people you care about.MagicBands can also be read by long-range readers to deliver amazing personalized experiences, as well as provide information that helps us improve the overall experience in our Resort. You don’t have to do anything beyond being nearby to interact with long-range readers. They just work—like magic! , In addition to touching your MagicBand or card to a touch point, you will be required to enter a PIN code to uniquely identify yourself when making purchases. To enter the parks, you will be required to provide biometric identification or show a photo ID that matches the name identified with your ticket. This process helps to ensure that you, and only you, have access to the entitlements linked to your MagicBand or card.MagicBands are always operational. They don’t have an on/off switch. If you lose a MagicBand, you can deactivate it on My Disney Experience, , and it will no longer be linked to your tickets and other entitlements.MagicBands use Radio Frequency (RF) technology and can be read by short and long-range readers located at the Walt Disney World Resort. If you prefer to use a card—which cannot be detected by long-range readers—you can request a card at your Disney Resort hotel.Please note: valid theme park admission is required to use FastPass+ service. In addition, any Guest who wishes to use their MagicBand to purchase an alcoholic beverage at Walt Disney World Resort must also present a valid form of identification.Learn about our privacy and data collection policies and the Radio Frequency (RF) technology used in MagicBands.
I do not live in the United States. Will you ship my MagicBand internationally?
Unfortunately, MagicBand orders cannot be shipped to all countries. When you customize your MagicBand, you’ll be asked to provide a shipping address. If, during this process, you discover that we do not ship to your country—but you plan on staying at a Disney Resort hotel, —your MagicBand will automatically be waiting for you at the Front Desk when you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel. Likewise, you can also arrange to have your MagicBand sent to a non-Disney Resort hotel with a valid shipping address prior to the start of your vacation.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.If you are a Passholder with an address where we do not ship, we ask that you provide us with an address where we can send your MagicBand at least 11 days before you plan to visit Walt Disney World Resort.If you have not yet done so, customize your MagicBand.
I purchased a MagicBand online or at a retail location. How do I link it to my Disney account so that I can use it?
If you purchased your MagicBand online at shopDisney,  or at a retail location, please follow these steps to link it to your Disney account:Create,  or sign into,  your Disney account.Link your MagicBand,  to your Disney account.To use your MagicBand with FastPass+ service, , both your MagicBand and valid theme park admission must be linked to your Disney account. If you have not already done so, please link your ticket, Annual Pass or package,  to your Disney account.
What should I do if I lose my MagicBand or card?
If you can access disneyworld.com, please visit the MagicBand section of My Profile,  and select the MagicBand or card you wish to deactivate. Then, when asked for the reason why you are deactivating, indicate that the MagicBand or card is lost. You can also deactivate a MagicBand by using the My Disney Experience mobile app.If you have another MagicBand or card available, you can activate it on the MagicBand section of My Profile.In the event that you lose your MagicBand or card while staying at Walt Disney World Resort, please visit Guest Relations,  or your Disney Resort hotel,  Lobby Concierge and we will deactivate it for you.Please note: On occasion, we may be able to provide you with a replacement MagicBand. However, replacement MagicBands are provided on a case-by-case basis and may be subject to a fee. In addition, limited-edition and specialty MagicBands cannot be replaced.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.Finally, If you’ve lost your MagicBand or card and your visit is still more than 11 days away, please contact us,  for assistance.Learn more about MagicBands.
My MagicBands did not arrive. What should I do?
If MagicBands have been shipped to you, fulfillment and shipping takes about 11 days, it might take a few days more or less depending on factors such as holidays, weekends and inclement weather.If MagicBands have been shipped to you, and they have not arrived and your visit to Walt Disney World Resort starts within 3 days, please contact us.If you do not receive your MagicBands before you travel to Walt Disney World Resort, you will be provided with MagicBands or cards when you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel.Replacement MagicBands may be subject to a fee.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.If you have not yet done so, customize your MagicBand.
How do I use my MagicBand or card when I have a FastPass+ arrival time at an attraction or entertainment experience?
As a result of the COVID-19 crisis, the FastPass+ service must be suspended as we plan to use additional queue space to control capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing. We will automatically cancel existing FastPass+ selections and share any future updates on the service at a later date.It’s so easy that you’ll think it’s magic!, When you arrive during your scheduled FastPass+,  arrival time, all you need to do is proceed to the FASTPASS queue entrance and touch your MagicBand or card to a sensor called a touch point.That’s it!, Please remember that each member of your party will have to individually touch their MagicBand or card to the touch point, so everyone should be sure to have their MagicBand or card available.Reserve access to FastPass+ attractions and entertainment.
I recently purchased an annual pass on disneyworld.com and have an exchange certificate. How do I customize and order my MagicBand?
If you have not already done so, please follow these steps to have your MagicBand shipped to your home:Create,  or sign into,  your Disney account.Link your annual pass or passes to your Disney account, . Your pass may have been linked automatically when you purchased it on disneyworld.com.If you are an Annual Passholder, you may activate your pass at any Walt Disney World theme park ticket window or Disney Springs Guest Relations,  location. Please bring your exchange certificate and a valid, government-issued photo ID, such as a driver's license or passport. Once your pass is activated upon first admittance into the theme parks, your MagicBand order will display in your Disney account.To order your MagicBands at pre-arrival prices, visit My MagicBands and Cards, . Remember to place your order at least 11 days before your arrival if you would like your MagicBands shipped to your home and at least 6 days before your arrival to have them shipped to your Resort hotel.Please note that one complimentary MagicBand will be available per each linked annual pass, and that MagicBand orders cannot be shipped to all countries.When you customize your MagicBand, the printed name appears on the inside for your privacy. Additionally, MagicBands that you purchase in the park or Disney Springs area will not have printed names, but you can select your preferred design or color.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.
My MagicBand or card does not work properly. What should I do?
If you are experiencing technical issues with your MagicBand,  or card—for example, if it is not recognized by a touch point—please ask the nearest Cast Member for assistance. If they are unable to correct the situation, please visit Guest Relations, , talk to a Disney Resort hotel,  Lobby Concierge or contact us.We will make sure to either get your MagicBand or card in proper working order or provide you with a replacement, so that you can continue to enjoy your visit to Walt Disney World Resort.Replacement MagicBands may be subject to a fee.
Are MagicBands waterproof?
Yes. MagicBands,  are waterproof so you don’t have to worry about protecting them from water exposure when you visit the Disney water parks, enjoy water attractions,  at the Disney theme parks, swim at the pool at your Disney Resort hotel,  or get caught outside in the rain.Valid theme park admission is required to use FastPass+ service.
Can I have multiple active MagicBands or cards?
Yes. If you have multiple MagicBands,  or cards linked to your Disney account, you can continue to use as many as your wrists and pockets can carry.However, getting multiple MagicBands or cards does not give you multiple entitlements, such as additional park admission. Also, once a MagicBand or card is linked to a person, it cannot be transferred to another person.You have the ability to manage which MagicBands and cards are active in My Profile, . Don’t see your MagicBand? You may need to link your Resort hotel reservation, link your Annual Pass,  or link the MagicBand,  to your Disney account.
I have multiple MagicBands or cards. How do I manage them?
You manage your MagicBands or cards in the MagicBand section of My Profile, . For example, you are able to:Activate or deactivate MagicBands or cards, Report a MagicBand or card as lost, Customize MagicBands before they are shipped, Multiple MagicBands or cards can be assigned to a single person, so activating a new MagicBand or card does not mean that you must deactivate an existing MagicBand or card. All active MagicBands or cards assigned to a person have access to the benefits and entitlements for that person. Adding a new MagicBand or card does not add new entitlements, such as additional theme park admissions.If you require additional assistance managing your MagicBands or cards, please contact us,  or visit any Guest Relations,  location at Walt Disney World Resort.
I have multiple Disney Resort hotel reservations. Will I receive multiple MagicBands?
If your arrival date is before December 31, 2020, you will receive a new MagicBand,  for every stay at a Disney Resort hotel,  and you can continue to use all of your active MagicBands. However, getting multiple MagicBands or cards does not give you multiple entitlements, such as additional FastPass+,  selections or park admission. Also, once a MagicBand or card is linked to a person, it cannot be transferred to another person.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.If you have multiple MagicBands or cards, you can manage which MagicBands and Cards are active in My Profile, . Don’t see your MagicBand? You may need to link your Resort hotel reservation, link your Annual Pass,  or link the MagicBand,  to your Disney account.
I am an Annual Passholder and my MagicBand did not arrive as scheduled or I forgot to bring it with me. What should I do?
Don’t worry, if your MagicBand,  did not arrive as scheduled or you did not bring it with you, you can still enjoy the Walt Disney World theme parks.Your Passholder card—with a photo ID—remains valid for theme park entry until it expires. You can use your MagicBand when you come back the next time!, If you do not have either your MagicBand or your Passholder card, please visit Guest Relations for assistance. Present a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport, to confirm your identity.Learn what to do if you believe that your MagicBand shipment was accidentally lost.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. Guests under age 18 must have parent or guardian permission to call.

With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.A MagicBand or card both allow you to enter the parks, unlock your Disney Resort hotel room and buy food and merchandise. Plus, your MagicBand or card gives you FastPass+,  access to all the experiences you’ve selected, so you can simply concentrate on enjoying the fun with the people you care about.Customizing your MagicBand is fun and easy, plus it’s a great way to differentiate your MagicBand from other members of your travel party. I am an Annual Passholder who is not currently a Guest of a Disney Resort hotel. Can I use my MagicBand to make purchases?
No. At this time, only Guests who are currently registered Guests at a Disney Resort hotel,  are able to use a MagicBand,  to charge purchases to their room—if they link the MagicBand to a credit card during check-in.However, your MagicBand allows you to enter the parks with your Annual Pass admission and link Disney PhotoPass,  photos to your Disney account.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. I am an Annual Passholder. Can I pick up my MagicBand the next time I visit Walt Disney World Resort?
Unfortunately, we are not able to provide Passholders with their MagicBands when they arrive at Walt Disney World Resort. However, getting your new MagicBand is easy! Just follow these simple steps:Create,  or sign into,  your Disney account.Link your annual pass or passes to your Disney account, . Please bring your exchange certificate and a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.Use your annual pass to enter a Walt Disney World theme park or water park.Customize your MagicBand.Once you have completed steps 1 through 5, your MagicBand will be delivered directly to your home. If you would like to use your MagicBand during your next Walt Disney World vacation, please be sure to complete these steps at least 11 days prior to your visit.If it is within 11 days of your next theme park visit or your MagicBand did not arrive as scheduled, you can still enjoy the Walt Disney World theme parks. Your Passholder card—with a photo ID—remains valid for theme park entry until it expires. I have a Disney Premier Passport. Do I receive a MagicBand?
If you have a Disney Premier Passport, , please follow these simple steps at least 11 days before you plan to visit Walt Disney World Resort and your MagicBand,  will be delivered straight to your home:Create,  or sign into,  your Disney account.Link your Disney Premier Passport to your Disney account, , if you have not already done so.Customize your MagicBand.Please continue to bring your Disney Premier Passport to both the Disneyland Resort and Walt Disney World Resort. You will need the Disney Premier Passport for admission to Disneyland Resort theme parks and for your Passholder discounts at both the Disneyland Resort and Walt Disney World Resort.MagicBand orders cannot be shipped to all countries.For more information, please call (407) WDW-PASS or (407) 939-7277—or use the Annual Passholder Help Form,  to email our dedicated Help Team with any questions you may have about your annual pass. How much does a MagicBand cost?
Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond. Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.If you want to purchase a MagicBand, they are available starting at $14.99 plus tax. Explore the variety of styles and designs offered online or at select retail locations at Walt Disney World Resort and beyond.Guests with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 can choose to upgrade their MagicBand at a special pre-arrival price—starting at $10 each.Learn more about MagicBands.
How can I get a MagicBand?
MagicBands,  are available to Walt Disney World Annual Passholders,  and Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.Guests can purchase a MagicBand:Online at shopDisney, Select Walt Disney World theme park and Resort hotel retail locations, Select Disney Springs retail locations, Other select merchandise and retail locations, MagicBands use Radio Frequency (RF) technology and can be read by short and long-range readers located at the Walt Disney World Resort. If you prefer to use a card—which cannot be detected by long-range readers—you can request a card at your Disney Resort hotel. MagicBands are not included with Water Parks Annual Passes. MagicBands and cards allow you to enter the parks, and unlock Disney Resort hotel rooms.Learn about our privacy and data collection policies and the Radio Frequency (RF) technology used in MagicBands.
How do I make purchases using my MagicBand?
If you’re staying at a Disney Resort hotel, , you can charge purchases to your room by touching your MagicBand or card against a sensor called a touch point and entering a PIN code to uniquely identify yourself. You self-select your PIN upon check-in at your Walt Disney World Resort hotel.Hungry for a snack? Want a souvenir? Use your MagicBand to charge these purchases at a Walt Disney World theme park to your Disney Resort hotel room. Plus, with valid theme park admission, use your MagicBand to check in at FastPass+ entrances and enjoy fun with the people you care about.If you haven’t yet, customize your MagicBand.
I did not receive a MagicBand from a Disney Resort hotel reservation or from an Annual Pass. Can I purchase a MagicBand?
Yes. You can purchase a MagicBand:Online at shopDisney, Select Walt Disney World theme park and Resort hotel retail locations, Select Disney Springs retail locations, Other select merchandise and retail locations, Link a MagicBand,  or link a theme park ticket,  to your Disney account.
I received my MagicBands, and there is something wrong with them. What should I do?
If there is something wrong with your MagicBands, —for example if your MagicBands are the wrong color or they are visibly broken—please contact us.Don’t worry! We’ll try to correct your issue as soon as possible and send you a replacement if necessary. If we cannot replace your MagicBands before you travel to Walt Disney World Resort, you will be provided with MagicBands or cards when you arrive at your Disney Resort hotel.Replacement MagicBands may be subject to a fee.If you have not yet done so, customize your MagicBand.Starting in 2021, we plan to unveil an innovative new offering as part of the My Disney Experience app that will bring features of a MagicBand to your smart devices. With this new offering, MagicBands will no longer be provided on a complimentary basis with new Disney Resort hotel reservations for Guests with arrivals beginning Jan. 1, 2021 and beyond.Guests staying at Disney Resort hotels with an arrival date through December 31, 2020 will receive complimentary MagicBands.
Can I use my MagicBand with special event tickets?
Yes. Your MagicBand can access special event tickets linked to your Disney account.Special events, such as Mickey's Not-So-Scary Halloween Party,  and Mickey's Very Merry Christmas Party, , can sell out quickly. Due to their popularity, we suggest that when you are planning your vacation to Walt Disney World Resort, you purchase tickets to events in advance.Link a ticket to your Disney account.
Can other people use my MagicBand or card?
No. Your MagicBand,  or card is unique to you and only you are authorized to access the benefits associated with it—including linked tickets, FastPass+ experiences, touch-to-pay purchases and other entitlements. Once a MagicBand or card is linked to your Disney account, it cannot be transferred to another person.In addition to touching your MagicBand or card to a touch point, you will be required to scan a finger to enter the parks or enter a PIN code to uniquely identify yourself when making purchases. This process helps to ensure that you, and only you, have access to the entitlements linked to your MagicBand or card.Please Check Our Property Rules, We ask that you review our Walt Disney World Resort property rules,  before your visit to avoid any delays or disruptions. We regularly update our property rules to ensure you have a safe and enjoyable experience at Walt Disney World Resort.If you have questions, please contact us.
What is a MagicBand?
Please note: As a result of the COVID-19 impact, FastPass+ service must be suspended for the time being, as we plan to use additional queue space to manage capacity at our attractions and maintain physical distancing.Tap into the magic with your MagicBand,  on your wrist. This colorful wristband is actually an all-in-one device that effortlessly connects you to all the vacation choices you made with My Disney Experience.Your MagicBand enables you to travel lighter throughout your vacation. Use it to enter the parks, unlock your Disney Resort hotel room and buy food and merchandise. Plus, your MagicBand gives you FastPass+,  access to all the experiences you’ve selected online, so you can simply concentrate on enjoying the fun with the people you care about.MagicBands add a touch of magic to your vacation by unlocking special surprises, personalized just for you, throughout the Walt Disney World Resort. Once you’ve linked your MagicBand, , you don’t need to do anything different. Your MagicBand and My Disney Experience profile will do the rest, creating unexpected Disney moments–just like magic.And, each of these magical moments will be transformed into a one-of-a-kind digital keepsake by Disney PhotoPass Service, . All you have to do is go to your PhotoPass account to see all the memories we’ve captured and created for you.Valid theme park admission is required to use FastPass+ service.Learn about our privacy and data collection policies and the Radio Frequency (RF) technology used in MagicBands.
How do I tell our MagicBands apart from each other?
Customized MagicBands,  can have different colors and art styles. If 2 or more have an identical color, look for a printed name or number on the inside of each MagicBand.In the MagicBand section of My Profile,  you can see the color and number of each person’s MagicBand. Only MagicBands that you manage will appear, so you may have to ask other people you are traveling with to sign in and view their MagicBands.If you still can’t tell your MagicBands apart, please visit any Guest Relations,  location, talk to a Disney Resort hotel,  Lobby Concierge or contact us.MagicBands that you purchase in the park or Disney Springs will not have printed names, but you can select your preferred color.If you have not yet done so, customize your MagicBand.
How do I view or download photos that I linked to my Disney account with my MagicBand?
Once you’ve linked your MagicBand to your My Disney Experience account, you can view your Disney PhotoPass pictures here.Be sure to link any MagicBands or cards, —including Memory Maker,  cards and Disney PhotoPass cards, —that you’ve used, while on your Walt Disney World vacation and at select Disney PhotoPass attraction and dining locations.Disney PhotoPass Service,  is the picture-perfect way to capture and share your magical vacation memories in great photos. Photographers are conveniently located around many of the most famous Disney icons, at most Disney Character meet-and-greet locations and even special Character dining locations.You can also purchase Memory Maker,  to gather photos of everyone,  in your travel party. Memory Maker includes all your Disney PhotoPass photos taken throughout the Walt Disney World Resort for one price, including select attraction and dining photos.
I have a Water Park After 2 Annual Pass. Do I receive a MagicBand?
No. Having a Water Park After 2 Annual Pass does not make you eligible to receive a MagicBand.However, if you already have a MagicBand—perhaps through a reservation at a Disney Resort hotel, —and both the MagicBand and unexpired Annual Pass are linked to your Disney account, , you are able to use the MagicBand to access the admission benefits of your Annual Pass to enter the Disney Water Parks.If you have not already received a new RF-enabled Water Park After 2 Annual Pass, you may need to exchange your older pass for a new card at the Disney’s Typhoon Lagoon Water Park,  or Disney’s Blizzard Beach Water Park,  ticket window.
Are you installing automatic cameras at character greetings?
We will be installing cameras at nine character greeting locations that will be in use beginning in early 2019. Multiple cameras will capture numerous memorable moments during a character interaction, allowing guests to choose from a wider variety of character photos.While Disney PhotoPass,  Cast Members will no longer capture photography at these nine locations, photographers will continue to support the more than 100 other Disney PhotoPass,  locations across our parks so that they can use their creativity to take personalized photos for our Guests.
I purchased Memory Maker. When can I begin downloading my photos?
With the My Disney Experience Mobile App,  or by visiting Disney PhotoPass, , you can begin downloading your Memory Maker photos as soon as they are available in your Disney account—or you can wait until you get home and download them all at once.Either way, you can download your photos as many times as you like until they expire—currently 45 days after the date the photo was taken.If you purchased Memory Maker at the advance purchase price, photos taken within 3 days of the date of purchase will not be included in Memory Maker and must be purchased separately.View your Memory Maker photos.
Can "friends of friends"—people connected to people in my Family & Friends list—also see my Disney PhotoPass photos?
No. Only Guests in your Family & Friends list,  who you have allowed access may view your Disney PhotoPass photos,  online at Disney PhotoPass,  or on the My Disney Experience Mobile App.To allow others to view the images in your Disney PhotoPass account, sign in to your Disney account and set photo sharing permissions using your Family & Friends list, . On your Family & Friends list, locate the Guest you want to share your photos with and select “Edit” to access the photo sharing control.Learn more about Disney PhotoPass.
I used my Disney PhotoPass photos to create gift products on the EZ Prints website. What should I do if I have a question or if there is a problem with my order?
Please call EZ Prints at (877) 651-4321 or visit their customer service webpage,  for all inquiries.
Why are some images missing from my Disney PhotoPass gallery when I view it on the EZ Prints website?
Certain properties and Characters that might be photographed at Walt Disney World Resort (such as Star Wars locations or Marvel Super Heroes) are protected by licensing arrangements that limit Disney’s ability to transfer certain images to a third party, such as EZ Prints. However, if you purchase and download your Disney PhotoPass photos from your Disney account, you will be able to print, share and create gift products with them for your personal use. For more details, see the Limited License referenced in the PhotoPass Terms and Conditions.
Does my Memory Maker purchase allow me to download photos linked to my family and friends?
Yes. You can download photos and videos from up to 25 members of your Family & Friends list,  that share photos taken during your Memory Maker,  window.Your Memory Maker window starts once you capture your first photo—or if you purchased Memory Maker at the advance purchase price, the Memory Maker window begins 3 days following the date Memory Maker was purchased—and ends 30 days following your first photo download or when you otherwise redeem your Memory Maker purchase.To view and download your Family & Friends’ photos, please ask them to sign in to their Disney account and set photo sharing permissions using your Family & Friends list, . On their Family & Friends list, they can locate the Guest they want to share photos with and select “Edit” to access the photo sharing control.Once the photos have been shared, you will be able to view, purchase and download them along with your Disney PhotoPass photos on Disney PhotoPass,  and on the My Disney Experience Mobile App.Also, if you there are more than 25 members of your Family & Friends list sharing images, you will need assistance to be able to share, view and download photos and videos from all of them at one time. Contact Disney PhotoPass Guest Support,  at (407) 560-4300 for these and any issues regarding missing photos. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.Photo sharing rules are subject to change.
Do the people on my Family & Friends list need to purchase Memory Maker to view my Disney PhotoPass photos?
No. You are free to share your photos on Disney PhotoPass,  and through the My Disney Experience Mobile App, —a Memory Maker purchase is not required for people on Family & Friends list,  to view your photos.Photo sharing is set one person at a time, so you control who is able to view the images linked to your Disney account. Guests who you allow to view your photos will also have the option to purchase prints, digital downloads or keepsakes of any of your photos.To allow others to view the photos linked to your Disney account, set photo sharing permissions using your Family & Friends list, . On your Family & Friends list, locate the Guest you want to share your photos with and select “Edit” to access the photo sharing control.If someone is not on your Family & Friends list and you do not wish to add them, you can also invite people to view your photos through email or Facebook.Learn more about Memory Maker.
What should I do if photos from members of my Family & Friends list are missing from my Disney PhotoPass gallery?
There are a few reasons you may be unable to see photos taken by someone on your Family & Friends list in your gallery.First, verify that this person has accepted your invitation to join your Family & Friends list. If so, confirm that they have enabled "Share My Disney PhotoPass Photos.”, Also, if there are more than 25 members of your Family & Friends list sharing images, you will need assistance to be able to share, view and download photos and videos from all of them at one time.Contact Disney PhotoPass Guest Support,  at (407) 560-4300 for these and any issues regarding missing photos. Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.
How do I link an attraction photo to my Disney account so that I am able to download it with my Memory Maker purchase?
Immediately after enjoying a participating attraction, visit the attraction’s Sales Center to link the photo by using any MagicBand or card, , Memory Maker card or Disney PhotoPass Card associated with your Disney account.You may also view and download attraction photos from up to 25 members of your Family & Friends list who share photos with you during your Memory Maker window. Once you’ve linked your photo, you can view, download and share your memories on Disney PhotoPass,  and on the My Disney Experience Mobile App.Learn more about Memory Maker.
I purchased Memory Maker after I took Disney PhotoPass photos. Will these photos be available for download as part of my Memory Maker purchase?
Photos that are linked to your Disney account—and have not expired—are included in your Memory Maker,  entitlement if you purchased Memory Maker at the regular purchase price. However, if you purchased Memory Maker at the advance purchase price, any photos taken within 3 days of the date of purchase are not included.See a photo you love—but it’s not eligible for download with Memory Maker? All available Disney PhotoPass photos are available for purchase as downloads or on a variety of unique photo gift and print products. Additional fees apply.View your Disney PhotoPass photos.
What is Memory Maker?
Memory Maker is an incredible new way to enjoy unlimited digital Disney PhotoPass,  photos captured at hundreds of locations throughout Walt Disney World Resort—including select attraction and dining locations. The photos are conveniently connected to your online Disney account with a touch of your MagicBand or card.You can conveniently view, download and share your Disney PhotoPass memories on Disney PhotoPass,  and on the My Disney Experience Mobile App.There’s no need to purchase each photo individually. You can simply enjoy your vacation knowing that your memories are being captured for you.Learn more about Memory Maker.Memory Maker includes photos taken during the Memory Maker window and linked to the Memory Maker Guest’s Disney account. Photos will expire pursuant to the expiration policy, . If Memory Maker is purchased at the advance purchase price, any photos taken within 3 days from the date Memory Maker is purchased will not be included and must be purchased separately. Not responsible for missing, lost or damaged photos. Subject to Memory Maker terms and conditions.
Some of my Disney PhotoPass photos are missing from my Disney account. What should I do?
Please link all of the MagicBands or cards,  that you may have used at Disney PhotoPass locations—including your annual pass, park ticket Memory Maker,  and Disney PhotoPass cards.If you still don’t see your photos, report a missing photo online,  or contact the Disney PhotoPass Guest Support team by calling (407) 560-4300.Guests under 18 years of age must have parent or guardian permission to call.View your Disney PhotoPass photos,  or with the My Disney Experience app.
How long will Memory Maker photos be available in my Disney account?
Disney PhotoPass photos, photos from select dining locations, photos from select attractions and any other media in your account are subject to the Disney PhotoPass Expiration Policy,  and currently expire 45 days from the date the photo was taken.You may be able to purchase an expiration extension on the Disney PhotoPass website.View your Disney PhotoPass photos.
How do I download my Memory Maker photos?
You can view your photos on Disney PhotoPass,  and on the My Disney Experience Mobile App!, Select your favorites and add them to your cart. Visit My Downloads,  and download as many photos—as many times—as you wish.You can download your Memory Maker photos right away through Disney PhotoPass,  and on the My Disney Experience app, —or you can wait until you get home and download them all at once.If you purchased Memory Maker in the park, you may need to link Memory Maker to your Disney account,  before you can begin downloading photos. You may also need to link any MagicBands or cards,  that you used at the Disney PhotoPass locations to view and download your photos.Learn more about Memory Maker.
I’ve purchased Memory Maker, taken photos at Walt Disney World Resort and linked them to my Disney account. How do I share my photos with other people? 
If you are the Guest who is assigned Memory Maker, you are able to download the photos on Disney PhotoPass,  and on the My Disney Experience Mobile App,  (with a limited license for personal, non-commercial use) at no additional cost. Once you’ve downloaded your photos to your computer or mobile device, you are free to share them however you wish—including by printing them at home, over email or through popular social media services like Facebook and Twitter.In addition, if you have connected with people through your Family & Friends list,  and shared photos with them, they can view your photos until the photos expire. To allow others to view the photos linked to your Disney account, visit your Family & Friends list, . On your Family & Friends list, locate the Guest you want to share your photos with and select “Edit” to access the photo sharing control.If someone is not on your Family & Friends list and you do not wish to add them, you can also invite people to view your photos through email.Learn more about Memory Maker.

Does Memory Maker include any physical photo prints or products?
Memory Maker,  is a digital-only entitlement. You can visit the Disney PhotoPass website,  to purchase prints, Disney Photo Gifts and other products using your Disney PhotoPass photos.
I have purchased Memory Maker. How do I manage which member of my group it is assigned to?
Before you download any photo or otherwise redeem your Memory Maker purchase, you can reassign the Memory Maker,  entitlement to any person who has a Disney account and who is connected to your Family & Friends list, . Once assigned, that individual will become the owner of the entitlement.To reassign Memory Maker, locate your Memory Maker in My Reservations,  in My Disney Experience,  and select the “Reassign” link.If you do not see Memory Maker in My Reservations, you may need to first link it to your Disney account.
Can I let other people view my Disney PhotoPass photos online?
Yes. Through Disney PhotoPass,  and the My Disney Experience Mobile App,  you may allow anyone who is connected to your Family & Friends list,  to view your photos. Photo sharing is set one person at a time, so you control who is able to view all the Disney PhotoPass photos,  connected to your Disney account. Guests who you allow to view your photos will also have the option to purchase prints, digital downloads or keepsakes of any of your photos.To allow others to view the images in your Disney PhotoPass account, sign in to your Disney account online at MyDisneyPhotoPass.com,  or on the My Disney Experience App,  and set photo sharing permissions using your Family & Friends list, . On your Family & Friends list, locate the Guest you want to share your photos with and select “Edit” to access the photo sharing control.If someone is not on your Family & Friends list and you do not wish to add them, you can also invite people to view your photos through email or Facebook.Learn more about Disney PhotoPass.
Can I restrict the people who can view my Memory Maker photos?
Yes. Photo sharing is set one person at a time, so you control who is able to view the images linked to your Disney account on Disney PhotoPass,  and the My Disney Experience Mobile App, . Guests who you allow to view your photos will also have the option to purchase prints, digital downloads, Disney Photo Gifts and other products using your Disney PhotoPass photos.To restrict others from viewing the photos linked to your Disney account, set photo sharing permissions using your Family & Friends list, . On your Family & Friends list, locate the Guest you want to share your photos with and select “Edit” to access the photo sharing control.Learn more about Memory Maker.
How do I change or disable the sharing settings that allow someone else to view my Disney PhotoPass photos?

Can I view the Disney PhotoPass photos of other people I am traveling with?

How long can I capture photos at Walt Disney World Resort with my Memory Maker purchase?
You can begin capturing photos as soon as you purchase Memory Maker. What happens when someone accepts my Family & Friends invitation for My Disney Experience?
Once you invite someone to connect to your Family & Friends list, that person will receive an email notification and be given the choice to accept or decline your invitation. When they accept, you will see a check mark next to their name in your Family & Friends list and you can then share the vacation planning activities in My Disney Experience. If you wish to modify what information you are sharing with other people, you can change your Family & Friends viewing permissions,  for each individual Guest by selecting the “Edit” button next to someone’s name in your Family & Friends list.View your Family & Friends list,  to invite someone to connect with you. You must sign in to My Disney Experience to view or modify your Family & Friends.
Do I have to link all of my tickets to my Disney account?
No. However, to take full advantage of MyMagic+, , we recommend that Guests link their tickets,  to their Disney account.Linking a ticket to your Disney account allows you to conveniently access your tickets through your MagicBand or card, , so you don’t have to worry about bringing multiple pieces of paper with you on your vacation. You can link theme park tickets, water park tickets, special event tickets and annual passes.Don’t worry! If you lose your MagicBand or card and it is linked to your Disney account, you do not also lose your tickets. You can request a replacement MagicBand or card,  and access your tickets through the new MagicBand or card. Replacement MagicBands may be subject to a fee.Please hold on to any annual pass that you link to your Disney account, as you may need to show your pass for theme park complimentary standard parking (if your pass includes parking) and food and merchandise discounts—along with a valid photo ID, such as a driver’s license or passport.
